CREATE TABLE "PAMPITE"."ALES"  ( 
	"ID"     	INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY (START WITH 1, INCREMENT BY 1, CACHE 20, MINVALUE 1, MAXVALUE 2147483647, CYCLE, ORDER) NOT NULL,
	"DTAES"  	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	"MBRID"  	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	"ACCTYPE"	CHARACTER(1) NOT NULL,
	"SUBACCT"	VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
	"GCM"    	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	"ABIGCM" 	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	"GCMMNEM"	CHARACTER(4) NOT NULL,
	"CLCODE" 	CHARACTER(10) NOT NULL,
	"QTY"    	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT "Q_PAMPITE_ALES_ID_00001" PRIMARY KEY("ID")
)
GO
CREATE TABLE "PAMPITE"."ALES_CONS"  ( 
	"ID"        	INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY (START WITH 1, INCREMENT BY 1, CACHE 20, MINVALUE 1, MAXVALUE 2147483647, CYCLE, ORDER) NOT NULL,
	"DTAES"     	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	"MBRID"     	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	"ACCTYPE"   	CHARACTER(1) NOT NULL,
	"GCM"       	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	"GCMACCTYPE"	CHARACTER(1) NOT NULL,
	"ABIGCM"    	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	"GCMMNEM"   	CHARACTER(4) NOT NULL,
	"QTY"       	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT "ALES_CONS_PK" PRIMARY KEY("ID")
)
GO
CREATE TABLE "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"  ( 
	"ST0DIV"  	CHARACTER(3) NOT NULL DEFAULT ' ',
	"ST0DAY"  	NUMERIC(4,0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"ST0TAS"  	NUMERIC(6,4) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"ST0TXOLD"	NUMERIC(6,4) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"ST0DATA" 	NUMERIC(8,0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"ST0ORA"  	NUMERIC(6,0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 
	)
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F" IS 'Prezzi di settlement - tabella tassi'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0DIV" IS 'CODICE ISO MONETA'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0DIV" TEXT IS 'CODICE ISO MONETA'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0DAY" IS 'NR. GG FASCIA'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0DAY" TEXT IS 'NR. GG FASCIA'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0TAS" IS 'TASSO INSERITO'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0TAS" TEXT IS 'TASSO INSERITO'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0TXOLD" IS 'TASSO PRECEDENTE'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0TXOLD" TEXT IS 'TASSO PRECEDENTE'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0DATA" IS 'DATA ULTIMA MOD'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0DATA" TEXT IS 'DATA ULTIMA MOD'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0ORA" IS 'ORA ULTIMA MOD'
GO
LABEL ON COLUMN "PAMPITE"."CCGPTAS00F"."ST0ORA" TEXT IS 'ORA ULTIMA MOD'
GO

	"CCLASS" 	CHARACTER(6) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"COFCOD" 	CHARACTER(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"CEXCH1" 	NUMERIC(2,0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"CMKT1"  	CHARACTER(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"CEXCH2" 	NUMERIC(2,0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"CMKT2"  	CHARACTER(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"CEXCH3" 	NUMERIC(2,0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"CMKT3"  	CHARACTER(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"CGROUP" 	CHARACTER(3) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"CCORR"  	DECIMAL(7,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"CUISYM" 	CHARACTER(6) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"CUCUSP" 	CHARACTER(12) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"CUICLP" 	DECIMAL(15,8) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"CUIPCL" 	DECIMAL(15,8) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"CPTYPE" 	CHARACTER(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"CDESC"  	CHARACTER(35) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"CMINRT" 	DECIMAL(15,8) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
	"CVAT"   	CHARACTER(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
	"CVINC"  	DECIMAL(4,0) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

	"COMMENT"   	VARCHAR(500) DEFAULT NULL,
	"CRLOG"     	CHARACTER(1000) DEFAULT NULL,
	"ANLOG"     	CHARACTER(1000) DEFAULT NULL,
	"PROPLOG"   	CHARACTER(1000) DEFAULT NULL,
	"UPDTYPE"   	CHARACTER(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'C',
	"UPDUSR"    	VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'SYSTEM',
	"UPDDATE"   	TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
	"ANNV"      	INTEGER DEFAULT NULL,
	"CRNV"      	INTEGER DEFAULT NULL,
	"ANNDAYSPER"	INTEGER DEFAULT NULL,
	"CRNDAYSPER"	INTEGER DEFAULT NULL,
	"ANPRGEXP1" 	INTEGER DEFAULT NULL,
	"CRPRGEXP1" 	INTEGER DEFAULT NULL,
	"ANPRGEXP2" 	INTEGER DEFAULT NULL,
	"CRPRGEXP2" 	INTEGER DEFAULT NULL,
	"ANSTRTYPE" 	CHARACTER(1) DEFAULT NULL,
	"CRSTRTYPE" 	CHARACTER(1) DEFAULT NULL,
	"CUSTOM"    	CHARACTER(1) DEFAULT 'F',
	CONSTRAINT "PMPXSTRA_PK" PRIMARY KEY("UPDID")
)
GO

CREATE TABLE "PAMPITE"."TRUNPAIR"  ( 
	"LASTUPDDT" 	TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
	"REPORTLEI" 	VARCHAR(28) NOT NULL,
	"OTHERLEI"  	VARCHAR(28) NOT NULL,
	"UTI"       	VARCHAR(49) NOT NULL,
	"INTERNALID"	VARCHAR(6) NOT NULL,
	"SOURCE"    	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	"CRT_DATE"  	VARCHAR(25) DEFAULT NULL 
	)
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVBINSTR" ( "CLASSID", "CLASSDESC", "DIVISCODE", "PROPMARGIN", "PROPCOVER", "ANNV", "ANNDAYSPER", "ANMARGIN", "ANCOVER", "SUSP", "PROPOSE", "CUSTOM", "COMMENT", "LASTDATE", "FIRSTDATE", "CURRMAR", "CURRVALFROM" FOR "CURRV00001", "CURRCOVER", "REALMARGT", "ANDATE", "ANDESC" )
AS
SELECT L.CLASSID, L.CLASSDESC, L.DIVISCODE, M.PROPMARGIN , M.PROPCOVER , M.ANNV , M.ANNDAYSPER , M.ANMARGIN ANMARGIN , M.ANCOVER ,M.SUSP, M.PROPOSE ,M.CUSTOM, M.COMMENT , M.ANLASTHISD AS LASTDATE , M.ANFRSTHISD AS FIRSTDATE , C.MARGIN CURRMAR , C.INIVDATE AS CURRVALFROM , C.COVER AS CURRCOVER , S.REALMARGT , A.ANDATE AS ANDATE , A.COMMENT AS ANDESC FROM PAMPITE.PMPTANREG A , PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS L INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLMAR M ON L.CLASSID = M.CLASSID INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTSETUP S ON S.DIVISCODE = L.DIVISCODE LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLMARH C ON M.CLASSID = C.CLASSID WHERE L.STATUS = 'E' AND NOT EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLMARH C1 WHERE C1.CLASSID = C.CLASSID AND C1.INIVDATE > C.INIVDATE ) AND NOT EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTANREG A1 WHERE A1.ANDATE > A.ANDATE ) 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVBINSTR" IS 'CLASS VIEW'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVBTBRCH" ( "CLASSID", "STATUS", "SIMMAR", "BREACHVAR", "INSTRID", "NV", "BTID", "USRBRCH", "USRDAYS", "USRCOV", "PCLPRICE", "CLPRICE", "PRICEDATE" )
AS
SELECT C.CLASSID, C.STATUS, C.USRMAR AS SIMMAR, 
	B.USRMAR AS BREACHVAR, B.INSTRID,B.NV, B.BTID, 
	B.USRBRCH, B.USRDAYS,B.USRCOV, 
	B.PCLPRICE,B.CLPRICE ,B.PRICEDATE 
	FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTCL C 
	INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTBRCH B ON C.CLASSID=B.CLASSID 
	WHERE ABS(B.USRMAR)>=C.USRMAR 
	AND NOT EXISTS ( 
	SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTBRCH B1 
	WHERE B.BTID=B1.BTID 
	AND B.CLASSID=B1.CLASSID 
	AND B.INSTRID=B1.INSTRID
	AND ABS(B1.USRMAR)>=C.USRMAR 
	AND B.USRBRCH<B1.USRBRCH) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVBTCOLL" ( "BTID", "STATUS", "BTDATE", "HPARR", "STARTDATE", "ENDDATE", "BREACHNUMB" )
AS
SELECT C.BTID, B.STATUS, B.LSTHISTDAT AS BTDATE, C.HPARR, C.STARTDATE, C.ENDDATE, COUNT(C.HCTCOVERED) AS BREACHNUMB 
	FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTCOLL C 
	INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBT B ON C.BTID = B.BTID AND B.DIVISCODE = 'K' 
	WHERE C.HCTCOVERED = 'F' 
	GROUP BY C.BTID, B.STATUS, B.LSTHISTDAT,C.HPARR, C.STARTDATE, C.ENDDATE 
	UNION 
	SELECT C.BTID, B.STATUS, B.LSTHISTDAT AS BTDATE, C.HPARR, C.STARTDATE, C.ENDDATE, 
	CASE WHEN COUNT(C.HCTCOVERED) > 0 THEN 0 END AS BREACHNUMB 
	FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTCOLL C 
	INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBT B ON C.BTID = B.BTID AND B.DIVISCODE = 'K' 
	WHERE C.HCTCOVERED = 'T' 
	AND NOT EXISTS ( 
	SELECT DISTINCT(BTID) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTCOLL C2 
	 WHERE HCTCOVERED = 'F' AND C2.BTID = C.BTID 
	) 
	GROUP BY C.BTID, B.STATUS, B.LSTHISTDAT,C.HPARR, C.STARTDATE, C.ENDDATE 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVBTMREP" ( "DIVISCODE", "BTID", "OBSDATE", "DAILYOBSER", "OBSERVNUMB", "TOTBREACHNUMB" FOR "TOTBR00001", "LASTYEARBR1" FOR "LASTY00001", "DAILYBREACHNUMB" FOR "DAILY00001", "MINCNFLEV" )
AS
(SELECT B.DIVISCODE, B.BTID, B.BTDATE AS OBSDATE, 
		COUNT(M.BTID) AS DAILYOBSER, 
		(SELECT COUNT(S.BTID) FROM PAMPITE.PMPXBTMMBS S 
		 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTM B1 ON B1.BTID = S.BTID 
			WHERE S.BTID <= B.BTID AND B1.DIVISCODE = B.DIVISCODE AND B1.STATUS = 'E' 
			AND B1.BTDATE IN 
		 (SELECT DISTINCT(DATE) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCALEND C WHERE DATE(C.DATE) <= DATE(B.BTDATE) AND C.MARKETCODE ='MTS' 
		 ORDER BY DATE DESC FETCH FIRST 380 ROWS ONLY) 
		) AS OBSERVNUMB, 
		(SELECT SUM(S.BREACHNUMB) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTMSTA S WHERE S.BTID = B.BTID) AS TOTBREACHNUMB, 
		(SELECT COUNT(S.BTID) FROM PAMPITE.PMPXBTMMBS S 
		 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTM B1 ON B1.BTID = S.BTID 
			WHERE S.BTID <= B.BTID AND B1.DIVISCODE = B.DIVISCODE AND B1.STATUS = 'E' 
			AND B1.BTDATE IN 
		 (SELECT DISTINCT(DATE) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCALEND C WHERE DATE(C.DATE) <= (DATE(B.BTDATE) - 18 MONTH) AND C.MARKETCODE ='MTS' 
		 ORDER BY DATE DESC FETCH FIRST 380 ROWS ONLY 
		 ) 
		) AS LASTYEARBR1, 
		(SELECT COUNT(S.BTID) FROM PAMPITE.PMPXBTMMBS S 
		 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTM B1 ON B1.BTID = S.BTID 
		 WHERE S.BTID = B.BTID AND S.RFCOVERED = 'F' 
		) AS DAILYBREACHNUMB, 
		STP.MINCNFLEV 
		FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTM B 
		INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPXBTMMBS M ON M.BTID = B.BTID 
		INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTMSP STP ON STP.DIVISCODE = B.DIVISCODE 
		WHERE 
		B.DIVISCODE = 'O' AND 
		B.STATUS = 'E' 
		GROUP BY B.BTID,B.DIVISCODE, B.BTDATE,STP.MINCNFLEV 
		UNION 
		SELECT B.DIVISCODE, B.BTID, B.BTDATE AS OBSDATE, 
		COUNT(M.BTID) AS DAILYOBSER, 
		(SELECT COUNT(S.BTID) FROM PAMPITE.PMPXBTMMBS S 
		 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTM B1 ON B1.BTID = S.BTID 
			WHERE S.BTID <= B.BTID AND B1.DIVISCODE = B.DIVISCODE AND B1.STATUS = 'E' 
			AND B1.BTDATE IN (SELECT DISTINCT(DATE) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCALEND C WHERE DATE(C.DATE) <= DATE(B.BTDATE) AND C.MARKETCODE ='MTA' 
			ORDER BY DATE DESC FETCH FIRST 380 ROWS ONLY)) AS OBSERVNUMB, 
		(SELECT SUM(S.BREACHNUMB) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTMSTA S WHERE S.BTID = B.BTID) AS TOTBREACHNUMB, 
		(SELECT COUNT(S.BTID) FROM PAMPITE.PMPXBTMMBS S 
		 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTM B1 ON B1.BTID = S.BTID 
			WHERE S.BTID <= B.BTID AND B1.DIVISCODE = B.DIVISCODE AND B1.STATUS = 'E' AND S.RFCOVERED = 'F' 
			AND B1.BTDATE IN (SELECT DISTINCT(DATE) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCALEND C WHERE DATE(C.DATE) <= (DATE(B.BTDATE) - 18 MONTH) AND C.MARKETCODE ='MTA' 
			ORDER BY DATE DESC FETCH FIRST 380 ROWS ONLY)) AS LASTYEARBR1, 
		(SELECT COUNT(S.BTID) FROM PAMPITE.PMPXBTMMBS S 
			 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTM B1 ON B1.BTID = S.BTID 
			 WHERE S.BTID = B.BTID AND S.RFCOVERED = 'F' 
		) AS DAILYBREACHNUMB, 
		STP.MINCNFLEV 
		FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTM B 
		INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPXBTMMBS M ON M.BTID = B.BTID 
		INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTMSP STP ON STP.DIVISCODE = B.DIVISCODE 
		WHERE 
		B.DIVISCODE != 'O' AND 
		B.STATUS = 'E' 
		GROUP BY B.BTID,B.DIVISCODE, B.BTDATE,STP.MINCNFLEV) 
		 --AS A 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVBTMSTA" ( "BTID", "OBSERVDATE", "DIVISCODE", "OBSERVNUMB", "BREACHNUMB", "DEFMINCNF", "CNFCOVERAGE" FOR "CNFCO00001", "CNFCOVERED" )
AS
SELECT B.*, CASE WHEN B.CNFCOVERAGE >= B.DEFMINCNF THEN 'T' ELSE 'F' END AS CNFCOVERED
FROM (
SELECT A.*, 
(DECIMAL(1-(DOUBLE(A.BREACHNUMB)/(DOUBLE(A.OBSERVNUMB))),15,8)) AS CNFCOVERAGE
FROM (SELECT
BTS.BTID,BTS.BTDATE AS OBSERVDATE, BTS.DIVISCODE, 
SUM(BTS.OBSERVNUMB) AS OBSERVNUMB, 
SUM(BTS.BREACHNUMB) AS BREACHNUMB,
BTS.MINCNFLEV AS DEFMINCNF
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTMSTA BTS 
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTM BTM ON BTM.BTID = BTS.BTID 
AND BTM.STATUS = 'E'
GROUP BY BTS.BTID,BTS.BTDATE, BTS.DIVISCODE,BTS.MINCNFLEV ORDER BY BTID DESC) AS A) AS B 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVBTSMCL" ( "CLASSID", "USRMAR", "STATUS", "DIVISCODE", "WORKMAR", "BTID", "BREACHES", "USRDAYS", "COVERAGE" )
AS
SELECT B.CLASSID, B.USRMAR, B.STATUS, B.DIVISCODE, 
	 C.USERMARGIN AS WORKMAR, 
	 R.BTID, 
	 COUNT(R.INSTRID)-1 AS BREACHES, 
	 MAX(R.USRDAYS) AS USRDAYS, 
	 (DECIMAL(MAX(R.USRDAYS))-DECIMAL(COUNT (R.INSTRID)-1))/DECIMAL(MAX(R.USRDAYS)) AS COVERAGE 
		FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTCL B 
	 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLMAR C ON B.CLASSID=C.CLASSID 
	 LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTBRCH R ON B.CLASSID=R.CLASSID 
	 WHERE 
	 B.USRMAR<=ABS(R.USRMAR) 
	 GROUP BY R.BTID,B.CLASSID, B.USRMAR, B.STATUS, B.DIVISCODE, C.USERMARGIN 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCATEG" ( "MARKETCODE", "CATEGORY", "INSTRTYPE", "TYPEDESC", "NUM" )
AS
SELECT I.MARKETCODE,C.CAT AS CATEGORY, T.INSTRTYPE, T.TYPEDESC,
	(
	SELECT COUNT(M.INSTRID)
	FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS M, PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I1
	WHERE TRUNC(M.MARGIN*20-0.000001,0)+1=C.CAT
	AND I1.INSTRID=M.INSTRID
	AND T.INSTRTYPE=I1.INSTRTYPE
	AND NOT EXISTS
		(SELECT *
		FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS V	
		WHERE V.INSTRID=I1.INSTRID
		AND V.INIVDATE>M.INIVDATE)
	) AS NUM
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTTYP T ,PAMPITE.PMPTMARCAT C, 
(SELECT DISTINCT INSTRTYPE,MARKETCODE 
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I
WHERE STATUS='E') AS I
WHERE T.INSTRTYPE=I.INSTRTYPE 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCHKCPR" ( "DATE", "INSTRID", "MARKETCODE", "FIRSTDATE", "LASTDATE" )
AS
SELECT C.DATE, I.INSTRID,I.MARKETCODE, E.FIRSTDATE, E.LASTDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCALEND C JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I ON I.MARKETCODE=C.MARKETCODE JOIN PAMPITE.PMPVEXTRPR E ON I.INSTRID=E.INSTRID WHERE DATE BETWEEN FIRSTDATE AND LASTDATE AND C.DATE NOT IN (SELECT P1.PRICEDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR P1 WHERE I.INSTRID=P1.INSTRID) 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVCHKCPR" IS 'COMPLETENESS HISTORICAL PRICE CHECK'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCHKCST" ( "INSTRID", "INSTRNAME", "CLASSCODE", "DIVISCODE", "MARKETCODE", "SGMCODE", "INSTRTYPE", "INSTRSTYPE", "CCPLSTDATE", "MKTLSTDATE", "NOTE", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "SENDDATE", "STATUS", "COMMENT", "SUSP", "MARCUSTOM", "MINCUSTOM", "STRACUSTOM" )
AS
SELECT I.INSTRID, I.INSTRNAME, I.CLASSCODE, I.DIVISCODE, I.MARKETCODE, I.SGMCODE, I.INSTRTYPE, I.INSTRSTYPE, I.CCPLSTDATE, I.MKTLSTDATE, I.NOTE, M.INIVDATE, M.ENDVDATE, M.SENDDATE, M.STATUS, M.COMMENT, M.SUSP, M.CUSTOM AS MARCUSTOM, D.CUSTOM AS MINCUSTOM, S.CUSTOM AS STRACUSTOM FROM PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMAR M ON I.INSTRID=M.INSTRID LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMINMAR D ON I.INSTRID=D.INSTRID LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTSTRA S ON I.INSTRID=S.INSTRID WHERE I.DIVISCODE IN ('E','D') AND M.STATUS='E' 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVCHKCST" IS 'CHECK CUSTOMIZED'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCLMAR" ( "CLASSID", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "SENDDATE", "STATUS", "CRMARGIN", "CRCOVER", "CRNDAYSPER", "CRNV", "ANMARGIN", "ANCOVER", "ANNDAYSPER", "ANNV", "USERMARGIN", "ANDATE", "PROPCOVER", "PROPMARGIN", "APPROVAL", "RCCODE", "COMMENT", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE", "PROPOSE", "CRLOG", "ANLOG", "PROPLOG", "USERCOV", "CRFRSTHISD", "ANFRSTHISD", "ANLASTHISD", "CRLASTHISD", "SUSP", "CUSTOM", "CRNODEID", "ANNODEID", "DIVISCODE", "CLASSDESC", "CLDIVIS", "WORKMAR", "WORKFROMDT", "CHMAR" )
AS
SELECT M.CLASSID, M.INIVDATE, M.ENDVDATE, M.SENDDATE, M.STATUS, M.CRMARGIN, M.CRCOVER, M.CRNDAYSPER, M.CRNV, M.ANMARGIN, M.ANCOVER, M.ANNDAYSPER, M.ANNV, M.USERMARGIN, M.ANDATE, M.PROPCOVER, M.PROPMARGIN, M.APPROVAL, M.RCCODE, M.COMMENT, M.UPDTYPE, M.UPDUSR, M.UPDDATE, M.PROPOSE, M.CRLOG, M.ANLOG, M.PROPLOG, M.USERCOV, M.CRFRSTHISD, M.ANFRSTHISD, M.ANLASTHISD, M.CRLASTHISD, M.SUSP, M.CUSTOM, M.CRNODEID, M.ANNODEID, M.DIVISCODE, C.CLASSDESC, C.DIVISCODE AS CLDIVIS, H.MARGIN AS WORKMAR, H.INIVDATE AS WORKFROMDT, (M.PROPMARGIN-H.MARGIN)/M.PROPMARGIN AS CHMAR FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLMAR M INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS C ON M.CLASSID=C.CLASSID LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLMARH H ON M.CLASSID=H.CLASSID WHERE NOT EXISTS( SELECT Z.INIVDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLMARH Z WHERE Z.INIVDATE>H.INIVDATE AND Z.INSTRID=H.INSTRID) 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVCLMAR" IS 'CLASS MARGINS'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCLSTAT" ( "INSTRID1", "INSTRID2", "CURVENAME1", "CURVENAME2", "INSTRNAME1", "INSTRNAME2", "CLASSID1", "CLASSID2", "CLASSDESC1", "CLASSDESC2", "DIVISCODE1", "DIVISCODE2", "NDAYSPER", "NV", "MODE", "CORREL", "PEARSON", "DIVUNDIV", "HISTDAYS" )
AS
SELECT S.INSTRID1, S.INSTRID2, I1.LISTNAME AS CURVENAME1, I2.LISTNAME AS CURVENAME2, I1.INSTRNAME AS INSTRNAME1, I2.INSTRNAME AS INSTRNAME2, S.CLASSID1, S.CLASSID2, C1.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDESC1, C2.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDESC2, I1.DIVISCODE AS DIVISCODE1, I2.DIVISCODE AS DIVISCODE2, S.NDAYSPER,S.NV, S.MODE, S.CORREL, S.PEARSON, S.DIVUNDIV, S.HISTDAYS FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLSTAT S INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I1 ON I1.INSTRID=S.INSTRID1 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I2 ON I2.INSTRID=S.INSTRID2 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS C1 ON C1.CLASSID=S.CLASSID1 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS C2 ON C2.CLASSID=S.CLASSID2 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCLTER" ( "DIVISCODE1", "CLASSDESC1", "CLASSID1", "DIVISCODE2", "CLASSDESC2", "CLASSID2", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "SENDDATE", "STATUS", "WORKSTATUS", "CROFF", "OFFSET", "CRINSTRID1", "CRINSTRID2", "CRNDAYSPER", "CRNV", "ANOFF", "ANINSTRID1", "ANINSTRID2", "ANNDAYSPER", "ANNV", "USEROFF", "ANDATE", "PROPOFF", "APPROVAL", "RCCODE", "COMMENT", "PROPOSE", "CRLOG", "ANLOG", "PROPLOG", "CRFRSTHISD", "ANFRSTHISD", "ANLASTHISD", "CRLASTHISD", "SUSP", "CUSTOM", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE" )
AS
SELECT 
	C1.DIVISCODE AS DIVISCODE1, 
	C1.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDESC1, T.CLASSID1, C2.DIVISCODE AS DIVISCODE2, C2.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDESC2, T.CLASSID2, 
	T.INIVDATE, T.ENDVDATE, T.SENDDATE, T.STATUS, H.STATUS AS WORKSTATUS,T.CROFF, 
	H.OFF AS OFFSET, T.CRINSTRID1, T.CRINSTRID2, T.CRNDAYSPER, T.CRNV, 
	T.ANOFF, T.ANINSTRID1, T.ANINSTRID2, T.ANNDAYSPER, T.ANNV, T.USEROFF, 
	T.ANDATE, T.PROPOFF, T.APPROVAL, T.RCCODE, T.COMMENT, T.PROPOSE, T.CRLOG, 
	T.ANLOG, T.PROPLOG, T.CRFRSTHISD, T.ANFRSTHISD, T.ANLASTHISD, 
	T.CRLASTHISD, T.SUSP, T.CUSTOM, T.UPDTYPE, T.UPDUSR, T.UPDDATE 
		FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTER T 
	 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS C1 ON C1.CLASSID = T.CLASSID1 
	 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS C2 ON C2.CLASSID = T.CLASSID2 
	 LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLTERH H ON H.CLASSID1 = T.CLASSID1 AND H.CLASSID2 = T.CLASSID2 
	 WHERE NOT EXISTS 
	(SELECT Z.INIVDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTERH Z WHERE Z.INIVDATE>H.INIVDATE AND Z.CLASSID1=H.CLASSID1 AND Z.CLASSID2 = H.CLASSID2) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCLTRA" ( "DIVISCODE", "CLASSDESC", "CLASSID", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "SENDDATE", "STATUS", "CROFF", "OFFSET", "CRINSTRID1", "CRINSTRID2", "CRNDAYSPER", "CRNV", "ANOFF", "ANINSTRID1", "ANINSTRID2", "ANNDAYSPER", "ANNV", "USEROFF", "ANDATE", "PROPOFF", "APPROVAL", "RCCODE", "COMMENT", "PROPOSE", "CRLOG", "ANLOG", "PROPLOG", "CRFRSTHISD", "ANFRSTHISD", "ANLASTHISD", "CRLASTHISD", "SUSP", "CUSTOM", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE" )
AS
SELECT 
	C.DIVISCODE AS DIVISCODE, 
	C.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDESC, T.CLASSID, 
	T.INIVDATE, T.ENDVDATE, T.SENDDATE, T.STATUS, T.CROFF, 
	H.OFF AS OFFSET, T.CRINSTRID1, T.CRINSTRID2, T.CRNDAYSPER, T.CRNV, 
	T.ANOFF, T.ANINSTRID1, T.ANINSTRID2, T.ANNDAYSPER, T.ANNV, T.USEROFF, 
	T.ANDATE, T.PROPOFF, T.APPROVAL, T.RCCODE, T.COMMENT, T.PROPOSE, T.CRLOG, 
	T.ANLOG, T.PROPLOG, T.CRFRSTHISD, T.ANFRSTHISD, T.ANLASTHISD, 
	T.CRLASTHISD, T.SUSP, T.CUSTOM, T.UPDTYPE, T.UPDUSR, T.UPDDATE 
		FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTRA T 
	 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS C ON C.CLASSID = T.CLASSID 
	 LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLTRAH H ON H.CLASSID = T.CLASSID 
	 WHERE NOT EXISTS 
	(SELECT Z.INIVDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTRAH Z WHERE Z.INIVDATE>H.INIVDATE AND Z.CLASSID=H.CLASSID) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCOLL" ( "INSTRID", "INSTRNAME", "LISTNAME", "CLASSCODE", "RICCODE", "ISINCODE", "BLOOMBCODE", "DIVISCODE", "MARKETCODE", "SGMCODE", "INSTRTYPE", "INSTRSTYPE", "CURRENCY", "DISABREAS", "ADDRSTREET", "ADDRCITY", "ADDRDIST", "ADDRPC", "ADDRSTATE", "ADDRCOUNT", "HISTPRID", "HISTVOLAID", "DELISTREAS", "DELISTDATE", "INDUSTRY", "COMPOS", "ISSUER", "DIVTYPE", "ADDRWEB", "BMKNAME", "BMKRIC", "BMKRETURN", "BMKSTYLE", "BMKAREA", "BMKDESCR", "BMKCOMP", "BMKSPEC", "BMKCURR", "BMKNINSTR", "STATUS", "FORMAT", "SHORTTFUT", "LONGTOPT", "FUTEXPNUMB", "MULT", "SHORTOPADJ", "DELDAYS", "IRNODE", "IRNODEDESC", "REPORTING", "NOTE", "MKTLSTDATE", "CCPLSTDATE", "SUPERSECT", "OPTEXPNUMB", "STRATYPE", "UNDINSTRID", "DEFHISTSER", "MARGINTH", "DERHIST", "MINMARTYPE", "EVTSTORMV", "DERPER", "DERFRSTMNT", "DERPRGMNT", "COMPARABLE", "RCCODE", "SETTLETYPE", "BNDCLASSID", "INTERP", "DURATION", "YIELD", "EXPIRY", "COUPNEXTDT", "COUPFREQ", "COUPTYPE", "COUPVAL", "MMTABLE", "DEFMARG", "DEFMINMAR", "DEFSTRADD", "PROCESS", "UPDTYPE", "UPDDATE", "UPDUSR", "CLASSDESC" )
AS
SELECT I.*, 
	CASE WHEN C.CNTRY IS NULL THEN BC.CLASSDESC ELSE HC.CLASSDESC END AS CLASSDESC --H.CLASSDESC 
	FROM PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I 
	LEFT JOIN 
	(SELECT DISTINCT(TRIM(COUNTRY)) AS CNTRY FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS) C ON I.LISTNAME = C.CNTRY 
	LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTHCLASS HC ON I.BNDCLASSID = HC.CLASSID 
	LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS BC ON I.BNDCLASSID = BC.CLASSID 
	WHERE I.DIVISCODE = 'K' 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCONF" ( "INSTRID", "NV", "NDAYSPER", "NDAYSDESC", "DEFCONF", "CONFIDENCE", "STATUS" )
AS
SELECT C.INSTRID,C.NV,D.NDAYSPER,D.NDAYSDESC, C.DEFCONF, (CASE C.DEFCONF WHEN 'T' THEN D.DEFCONFID ELSE C.CONFIDENCE END) AS CONFIDENCE, (CASE C.DEFCONF WHEN 'T' THEN D.DEFSTATUS ELSE C.STATUS END) AS STATUS FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCONF C,PAMPITE.PMPVCONFDF D WHERE D.INSTRID=C.INSTRID AND D.NV=C.NV AND D.NDAYSPER=C.NDAYSPER 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVCONF" IS 'ACTUAL CONFIDENCE PER INSTR. CONS. DEFAULT'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCONFDF" ( "INSTRID", "INSTRTYPE", "NV", "NDAYSPER", "NDAYSDESC", "DEFSTATUS", "DEFCONFID" )
AS
SELECT "I"."INSTRID", "I"."INSTRTYPE", "D"."NV", "P"."NDAYSPER", "PD"."NDAYSDESC", CASE DSTATUS WHEN 'D' THEN 'D' ELSE PSTATUS END AS "DEFSTATUS", "C"."CONFIDDF" AS "DEFCONFID" FROM PAMPITE.PMPTDELTDF "D" INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCONFDF "C" ON "D"."NV" = "C"."NV" INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR "I" ON "I"."INSTRTYPE" = "D"."INSTRTYPE" AND "I"."INSTRTYPE" = "C"."INSTRTYPE" INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTPERDF "P" ON "I"."INSTRTYPE" = "P"."INSTRTYPE" AND "P"."NDAYSPER" = "C"."NDAYSPER" INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTPER "PD" ON "PD"."NDAYSPER" = "P"."NDAYSPER" 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVCONFDF" IS 'DEFAULT CONFIDENCE PER INSTR.'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCSBNKGR" ( "BNKGRID", "MBRBNKGRNM" )
AS
SELECT DISTINCT(BNKGRID), S.MBRBNKGRNM FROM PAMPUAT.PMPTBNKGTC C
INNER JOIN 
(SELECT DISTINCT(MBRBNKGRID), MBRBNKGRNM FROM PAMPUAT.PMPTSTBNKS
) S
ON C.BNKGRID = S.MBRBNKGRID 
GO
RENAME TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVCSBNKGR" TO SYSTEM NAME "PMPVC00001"
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCSTCNF" ( "INSTRID", "INSTRNAME", "LISTNAME", "CLASSCODE", "RICCODE", "ISINCODE", "BLOOMBCODE", "DIVISCODE", "MARKETCODE", "SGMCODE", "INSTRTYPE", "INSTRSTYPE", "CURRENCY", "DISABREAS", "ADDRSTREET", "ADDRCITY", "ADDRDIST", "ADDRPC", "ADDRSTATE", "ADDRCOUNT", "HISTPRID", "HISTVOLAID", "DELISTREAS", "DELISTDATE", "INDUSTRY", "COMPOS", "ISSUER", "DIVTYPE", "ADDRWEB", "BMKNAME", "BMKRIC", "BMKRETURN", "BMKSTYLE", "BMKAREA", "BMKDESCR", "BMKCOMP", "BMKSPEC", "BMKCURR", "BMKNINSTR", "STATUS", "FORMAT", "SHORTTFUT", "LONGTOPT", "FUTEXPNUMB", "MULT", "SHORTOPADJ", "DELDAYS", "IRNODE", "IRNODEDESC", "REPORTING", "NOTE", "UPDTYPE", "UPDDATE", "UPDUSR", "MKTLSTDATE", "CCPLSTDATE", "SUPERSECT", "OPTEXPNUMB", "STRATYPE", "UNDINSTRID", "DEFHISTSER", "MARGINTH", "DERHIST", "MINMARTYPE", "COMPARABLE", "RCCODE", "SETTLETYPE", "BNDCLASSID", "DURATION", "MMTABLE", "DEFMARG", "DEFCONF" )
AS
SELECT I.INSTRID, I.INSTRNAME, I.LISTNAME, I.CLASSCODE, I.RICCODE, I.ISINCODE, I.BLOOMBCODE, I.DIVISCODE, I.MARKETCODE, I.SGMCODE, I.INSTRTYPE, I.INSTRSTYPE, I.CURRENCY, I.DISABREAS, I.ADDRSTREET, I.ADDRCITY, I.ADDRDIST, I.ADDRPC, I.ADDRSTATE, I.ADDRCOUNT, I.HISTPRID, I.HISTVOLAID, I.DELISTREAS, I.DELISTDATE, I.INDUSTRY, I.COMPOS, I.ISSUER, I.DIVTYPE, I.ADDRWEB, I.BMKNAME, I.BMKRIC, I.BMKRETURN, I.BMKSTYLE, I.BMKAREA, I.BMKDESCR, I.BMKCOMP, I.BMKSPEC, I.BMKCURR, I.BMKNINSTR, I.STATUS, I.FORMAT, I.SHORTTFUT, I.LONGTOPT, I.FUTEXPNUMB, I.MULT, I.SHORTOPADJ, I.DELDAYS, I.IRNODE, I.IRNODEDESC, I.REPORTING, I.NOTE, I.UPDTYPE, I.UPDDATE, I.UPDUSR, I.MKTLSTDATE, I.CCPLSTDATE, I.SUPERSECT, I.OPTEXPNUMB, I.STRATYPE, I.UNDINSTRID, I.DEFHISTSER, I.MARGINTH, I.DERHIST, I.MINMARTYPE, I.COMPARABLE, I.RCCODE, I.SETTLETYPE, I.BNDCLASSID, I.DURATION, I.MMTABLE, I.DEFMARG , (SELECT MIN(DEFCONF) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCONF C WHERE I.INSTRID=C.INSTRID) AS DEFCONF FROM PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCURGR" ( "GRID", "PGNAME", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "COEFF", "SENT", "SENDDATE", "RCCODE", "COMMENT", "APPROVEDBY", "APPRDATE", "ANCOEFF", "ANDATE", "LOG", "STATUS", "DIVISCODE", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE" )
AS
SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTGRHIST T WHERE INIVDATE>= ALL( SELECT INIVDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTGRHIST I WHERE I.GRID=T.GRID) 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVCURGR" IS 'LAST HISTORICAL GROUP'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVCURMAR" ( "INSTRID", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "MARGIN", "COVER", "MINMARGIN", "SENT", "SENDDATE", "APPROVEDBY", "APPRDATE", "ANMARBUFF", "ANNBMAR", "ANCAP", "ANMINMAR", "ANMARGIN", "ANCOVER", "ANDATE", "RCCODE", "COMMENT", "CLASSID", "LOG", "STRADDLE", "ANSTRADDLE", "SUSP", "MUL", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE" )
AS
SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS T WHERE INIVDATE>= ALL( SELECT INIVDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS I WHERE I.INSTRID=T.INSTRID) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVDINSTR" ( "INSTRID", "CLASSCODE", "INSTRNAME", "INSTRTYPE", "DIVISCODE", "SGMCODE", "MARKETCODE", "INDUSTRY", "MULT", "PROPMARGIN", "PROPCOVER", "ANNV", "ANNDAYSPER", "ANMARGIN", "ANCOVER", "SUSP", "PROPOSE", "COMMENT", "CUSTOM", "ANMINMAR", "USRMINMAR", "PROPMINMAR", "MPROPOSE", "ANSTRA", "USRSTRA", "PROPSTRA", "SPROPOSE", "LASTPR", "LASTDATE", "FIRSTPR", "FIRSTDATE", "CURRMAR", "CURRMINMAR", "CURRSTRADDLE" FOR "CURRS00001", "CURRVALFROM" FOR "CURRV00001", "CURRCOVER", "CURRMUL", "REALMARGT", "CURRMULT", "ANDATE", "ANDESC" )
AS
( SELECT T.INSTRID , T.CLASSCODE , T.INSTRNAME , T.INSTRTYPE, T.DIVISCODE , T.SGMCODE , T.MARKETCODE , T.INDUSTRY , T.MULT , M.PROPMARGIN , M.PROPCOVER , M.ANNV , M.ANNDAYSPER , M.ANMARGIN * 100 ANMARGIN , M.ANCOVER , M.SUSP, M.PROPOSE , M.COMMENT , M.CUSTOM, MIN.ANMINMAR , MIN.USRMINMAR , MIN.PROPMINMAR , MIN.PROPOSE AS MPROPOSE , STR.ANSTRA , STR.USRSTRA , STR.PROPSTRA , STR.PROPOSE AS SPROPOSE , P.CLOSEPR AS LASTPR , M.ANLASTHISD AS LASTDATE , F.CLOSEPR AS FIRSTPR , M.ANFRSTHISD AS FIRSTDATE , C.MARGIN * 100 CURRMAR , C.MINMARGIN AS CURRMINMAR , C.STRADDLE AS CURRSTRADDLE , C.INIVDATE AS CURRVALFROM , C.COVER AS CURRCOVER , C.MUL AS CURRMUL, S.REALMARGT , C.MUL AS CURRMULT, A.ANDATE AS ANDATE , A.COMMENT AS ANDESC FROM PAMPITE.PMPTANREG A , PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR T INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMAR M ON T.INSTRID = M.INSTRID INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTSETUP S ON T.DIVISCODE = S.DIVISCODE LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR P ON ( CASE WHEN ( T.DERHIST = 'F' OR T.DERHIST IS NULL ) THEN T.UNDINSTRID ELSE T.INSTRID END ) = P.INSTRID AND M.ANLASTHISD = P.PRICEDATE LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR F ON ( CASE WHEN ( T.DERHIST = 'F' OR T.DERHIST IS NULL ) THEN T.UNDINSTRID ELSE T.INSTRID END ) = F.INSTRID AND M.ANFRSTHISD = F.PRICEDATE LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMINMAR MIN ON T.INSTRID = MIN.INSTRID LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTSTRA STR ON T.INSTRID = STR.INSTRID LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS C ON T.INSTRID = C.INSTRID WHERE T.STATUS = 'E' AND T.DIVISCODE = 'D' AND NOT EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS C1 WHERE C1.INSTRID = C.INSTRID AND C1.INIVDATE > C.INIVDATE ) AND NOT EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTANREG A1 WHERE A1.ANDATE > A.ANDATE ) ) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVEXTRDE" ( "INSTRID", "FIRSTDATE", "LASTDATE", "NUM" )
AS
SELECT INSTRID, MIN(PRICEDATE) AS FIRSTDATE, MAX(PRICEDATE) AS LASTDATE, COUNT(PRICEDATE) AS NUM FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISDE GROUP BY INSTRID 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVEXTRPR" ( "INSTRID", "FIRSTDATE", "LASTDATE", "NUM" )
AS
SELECT INSTRID, MIN(PRICEDATE) AS FIRSTDATE, MAX(PRICEDATE) AS LASTDATE,COUNT(PRICEDATE) AS NUM FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR GROUP BY INSTRID 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVEXTRPR" IS 'FIRST/LAST HISTORICAL DATE FOR DER. INSTR.'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVFIRSTPR" ( "INSTRID", "PRICEDATE", "CLOSEPR", "STATUS", "UPDTYPE", "UPDDATE", "UPDUSR" )
AS
SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR T WHERE PRICEDATE<= ALL( SELECT PRICEDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR I WHERE I.INSTRID=T.INSTRID) 
GO
RENAME TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVFIRSTPR" TO SYSTEM NAME "PMPVF00001"
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVFIRSTPR" IS 'FIRST ROW OF HISTORICAL PRICES PER INSTR.'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVFSTPRD" ( "INSTRID", "PRICEDATE", "PC", "STRIKE", "EXPIRY", "CODE", "STATUS", "CLOSEPR", "IMPVOLA", "UPDDATE", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR" )
AS
SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISDE T WHERE PRICEDATE<= ALL( SELECT PRICEDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISDE I WHERE I.INSTRID=T.INSTRID) 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVFSTPRD" IS 'FIRST ROW OF DERIVATIVES HIST. PRICES PER INSTR'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVGRSTAT" ( "SETNAME", "DIVISCODE", "INSTRNAME1", "INSTRNAME2", "INSTRID1", "INSTRID2", "NDAYSPER", "NDAYSDESC", "NV", "VARTYPE", "MODE", "ACTIVE", "CORREL", "PEARSON", "DIVUNDIV", "SLOPE", "RELPERF", "TRACKERR", "HISTDAYS", "SETID", "STATUS", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE" )
AS
SELECT T.SETNAME, T.DIVISCODE, I1.INSTRNAME AS INSTRNAME1, I2.INSTRNAME AS INSTRNAME2, S.INSTRID1, S.INSTRID2, S.NDAYSPER,P.NDAYSDESC, S.NV, S.VARTYPE, S.MODE, S.ACTIVE, S.CORREL, S.PEARSON, S.DIVUNDIV, S.SLOPE, S.RELPERF, S.TRACKERR, S.HISTDAYS, S.SETID, S.STATUS, S.UPDTYPE, S.UPDUSR, S.UPDDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTGRSTAT S INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTSETS T ON T.SETID = S.SETID INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I1 ON S.INSTRID1 = I1.INSTRID INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I2 ON S.INSTRID2 = I2.INSTRID INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTPER P ON S.NDAYSPER=P.NDAYSPER 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVGRSTAT" IS 'GROUP STATISTICS WITH WITH DETAILS'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVHISV" ( "INSTRID", "PRICEDATE", "CLOSEPR", "CLOSEPRRET", "NV", "STATUS", "VARIAT", "ABSVARIAT", "HISTVOLA", "PRGEXP", "IMPVOLA", "PC", "MARGIN", "KCOEFF", "INVK", "FRSTEXDATE", "CATYPE" )
AS
SELECT P.INSTRID,P.PRICEDATE,P.CLOSEPR,PR.CLOSEPRRET, VA.NV, VA.STATUS, VA.VARIAT, ABS(VA.VARIAT) AS ABSVARIAT, VO.VARIAT AS HISTVOLA, DE.PRGEXP, DE.IMPVOLA, DE.PC, ( SELECT MARGIN FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS M WHERE P.INSTRID=M.INSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE>=M.INIVDATE ORDER BY M.INIVDATE DESC FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY ) AS MARGIN, CA.KCOEFF, CA.INVK, CA.FRSTEXDATE, CA.CATYPE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR P LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTHISPRR PR ON P.INSTRID=PR.INSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE=PR.PRICEDATE LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTVAR VA ON P.INSTRID=VA.INSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE=VA.PRICEDATE AND VA.VARTYPE='P' LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTVAR VO ON P.INSTRID=VO.INSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE=VO.PRICEDATE AND VA.NV=VO.NV AND VO.VARTYPE='V' LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCORPAC CA ON P.INSTRID=CA.INSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE=CA.FRSTEXDATE LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPVVOLA DE ON P.INSTRID=DE.UNDINSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE=DE.PRICEDATE 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVHISVBO" ( "INSTRID", "PRICEDATE", "IR", "PRICE", "NV", "STATUS", "IRVAR", "ABSIRVAR", "PRICEVAR", "ABSPRICEVAR" FOR "ABSPR00001", "HISTVOLA" )
AS
SELECT P.INSTRID,P.PRICEDATE,P.CLOSEPR AS IR, PR.CLOSEPRRET AS PRICE, VA.NV, VA.STATUS, VA.VARIAT AS IRVAR, ABS(VA.VARIAT) AS ABSIRVAR, VG.VARIAT AS PRICEVAR, ABS(VG.VARIAT) AS ABSPRICEVAR, VO.VARIAT AS HISTVOLA FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR P LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTHISPRR PR ON P.INSTRID=PR.INSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE=PR.PRICEDATE LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTVAR VA ON P.INSTRID=VA.INSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE=VA.PRICEDATE AND VA.VARTYPE='P' LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTVAR VO ON P.INSTRID=VO.INSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE=VO.PRICEDATE AND VA.NV=VO.NV AND VO.VARTYPE='V' LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTVAR VG ON P.INSTRID=VG.INSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE=VG.PRICEDATE AND VA.NV=VG.NV AND VG.VARTYPE='G' 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVHISVDE" ( "INSTRID", "DERHIST", "PRICEDATE", "PRGEXP", "STATUS", "CLOSEPRRET", "UCLOSEPRRET" FOR "UCLOS00001", "NV", "VARIAT", "HISTVOLA", "MARGIN" )
AS
SELECT I.INSTRID,I.DERHIST, VA.PRICEDATE, VA.PRGEXP, VA.STATUS, P.CLOSEPRRET, PU.CLOSEPRRET AS UCLOSEPRRET ,VA.NV, VA.VARIAT, VO.VARIAT AS HISTVOLA, (SELECT MARGIN FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS M WHERE I.INSTRID=M.INSTRID AND VA.PRICEDATE>=M.INIVDATE ORDER BY M.INIVDATE DESC FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY ) AS MARGIN FROM PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTVAR VA ON VA.INSTRID=(CASE WHEN I.DERHIST='T' THEN I.INSTRID ELSE I.UNDINSTRID END) AND VA.VARTYPE='P' LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTVAR VO ON VA.INSTRID=VO.INSTRID AND VA.PRICEDATE=VO.PRICEDATE AND VA.NV=VO.NV AND VO.VARTYPE='V' AND VA.PRGEXP=VO.PRGEXP LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTHISDER P ON P.INSTRID=VA.INSTRID AND P.PRICEDATE=VA.PRICEDATE AND P.PRGEXP=VA.PRGEXP LEFT OUTER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTHISPRR PU ON PU.INSTRID=VA.INSTRID AND PU.PRICEDATE=VA.PRICEDATE 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVIMPVOL" ( "CASHINSTRI", "INSTRID", "PRICEDATE", "PC", "STRIKE", "EXPIRY", "CODE", "STATUS", "CLOSEPR", "IMPVOLA", "UPDDATE", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR" )
AS
SELECT I.UNDINSTRID AS CASHINSTRI, D.INSTRID, D.PRICEDATE, D.PC, D.STRIKE, D.EXPIRY, D.CODE, D.STATUS, D.CLOSEPR, D.IMPVOLA, D.UPDDATE, D.UPDTYPE, D.UPDUSR 
		 
		FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISDE D 
		INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I ON D.INSTRID=I.INSTRID 
		 
		WHERE D.PC='C' 
		AND 1=( 
		 SELECT COUNT(*) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISDE D1 
		 WHERE D.INSTRID=D1.INSTRID 
		 AND D.PRICEDATE=D1.PRICEDATE 
		 AND D.PC=D1.PC 
		 AND D.EXPIRY>D1.EXPIRY) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVINSSEL" ( "CINSTRID", "CINSTRNAME", "CLISTNAME", "CCLASSCODE", "CRICCODE", "CISINCODE", "CIRNODE", "CDIVISCODE" )
AS
SELECT INSTRID AS CINSTRID, INSTRNAME AS CINSTRNAME, LISTNAME AS CLISTNAME, CLASSCODE AS CCLASSCODE, RICCODE AS CRICCODE, ISINCODE AS CISINCODE, IRNODE AS CIRNODE, DIVISCODE AS CDIVISCODE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVINSTR" ( "INSTRID", "CLASSCODE", "INSTRNAME", "INSTRTYPE", "DIVISCODE", "SGMCODE", "MARKETCODE", "INDUSTRY", "MULT", "PROPMARGIN", "PROPCOVER", "ANNV", "ANNDAYSPER", "PROPMINMAR", "ANMARGIN", "ANCOVER", "SUSP", "PROPOSE", "CUSTOM", "COMMENT", "LASTPR", "LASTDATE", "FIRSTPR", "FIRSTDATE", "CURRMAR", "CURRMINMAR", "CURRVALFROM" FOR "CURRV00001", "CURRCOVER", "REALMARGT", "ANDATE", "ANDESC" )
AS
SELECT T.INSTRID , T.CLASSCODE , T.INSTRNAME ,T.INSTRTYPE, T.DIVISCODE , T.SGMCODE , T.MARKETCODE , T.INDUSTRY , T.MULT , M.PROPMARGIN , M.PROPCOVER , M.ANNV , M.ANNDAYSPER , M.PROPMINMAR , M.ANMARGIN * 100 ANMARGIN , M.ANCOVER ,M.SUSP, M.PROPOSE , M.CUSTOM, M.COMMENT , P.CLOSEPR AS LASTPR , P.PRICEDATE AS LASTDATE , F.CLOSEPR AS FIRSTPR , F.PRICEDATE AS FIRSTDATE , C.MARGIN * 100 CURRMAR , C.MINMARGIN AS CURRMINMAR , C.INIVDATE AS CURRVALFROM , C.COVER AS CURRCOVER , S.REALMARGT , A.ANDATE AS ANDATE , A.COMMENT AS ANDESC FROM PAMPITE.PMPTANREG A , PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR T INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMAR M ON T.INSTRID = M.INSTRID INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTSETUP S ON T.DIVISCODE = S.DIVISCODE LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR P ON T.INSTRID = P.INSTRID AND M.ANLASTHISD = P.PRICEDATE LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR F ON T.INSTRID = F.INSTRID AND M.ANFRSTHISD = F.PRICEDATE LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS C ON T.INSTRID = C.INSTRID WHERE T.STATUS = 'E' AND NOT EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS C1 WHERE C1.INSTRID = C.INSTRID AND C1.INIVDATE > C.INIVDATE) AND NOT EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTANREG A1 WHERE A1.ANDATE > A.ANDATE ) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVIOSCOBT" ( "DIVISCODE", "OBSNUMB", "BREACH_NUMB" FOR "BREAC00001", "MAXUNCOVLOSS" FOR "MAXUN00001", "AVGUNCOVLOSS" FOR "AVGUN00001", "EXECNUMB", "EXECTIME", "CNFLV" )
AS
SELECT A.*, 
	DECIMAL((1.0-(1.0)*(A.BREACH_NUMB)/(A.OBSNUMB)),15,8) AS CNFLV 
	FROM 
	( 
	 SELECT BT.DIVISCODE, COUNT(*) AS OBSNUMB,SUM(CASE WHEN M.RFCOVERED='F' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS BREACH_NUMB, 
	 MAX(CASE WHEN M.RFCOVERED='F' THEN GAINLOSS ELSE 0 END) AS MAXUNCOVLOSS, 
	 SUM(CASE WHEN M.RFCOVERED='F' THEN GAINLOSS ELSE 0 END)/(SUM(CASE WHEN M.RFCOVERED='F' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)) AS AVGUNCOVLOSS, 
	 BTMS.EXECNUMB, 
	 BTMS.EXECTIME 
	 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTM BT 
	 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPXBTMMBS M ON M.BTID = BT.BTID 
	 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTMSP BTMS ON BT.DIVISCODE = BTMS.DIVISCODE 
	 WHERE BT.STATUS = 'E' AND M.REFDATE >= (NOW() - 1 YEAR) 
	 GROUP BY BT.DIVISCODE,BTMS.EXECNUMB,BTMS.EXECTIME 
	) AS A 
GO
RENAME TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVIOSCOBT" TO SYSTEM NAME "PMPVI00001"
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVIOSCOCLE" ( "DIVISCODE", "MBRDESC", "OBSNUMB", "BREACH_NUMB" FOR "BREAC00001", "EXECNUMB", "EXECTIME", "CNFLV" )
AS
SELECT A.*,
DECIMAL((1.0-(1.0)*(A.BREACH_NUMB)/(A.OBSNUMB)),15,8) AS CNFLV
FROM (
SELECT 'O' AS DIVISCODE, M.MBRDESC, COUNT(*) AS OBSNUMB,
SUM(CASE WHEN M.RFCOVERED='F' AND M.GAINLOSS > GRRMAR.AMOUNT THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS BREACH_NUMB,
BTMS.EXECNUMB, 
BTMS.EXECTIME
FROM PAMPITE.PMPXBTMMBS M
INNER JOIN GRR.LSEG_MAR GRRMAR ON GRRMAR.MEMBER_MNEMONIC = 'CLEA' AND GRRMAR.MARGIN_TYPE = 'ADD_INT_MA' AND GRRMAR.BUSINESS_TIMESTAMP = INT(REPLACE(CHAR(DATE(M.REFDATE), ISO),'-',''))
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTBTMSP BTMS ON BTMS.DIVISCODE = 'O'
WHERE M.MBRID = 1323
AND M.REFDATE >= (NOW() - 1 YEAR)
GROUP BY M.MBRDESC,BTMS.EXECNUMB, 
BTMS.EXECTIME) AS A 
GO
RENAME TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVIOSCOCLE" TO SYSTEM NAME "PMPVI00002"
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVIOSCOST" ( "DIVISCODE", "BNKRANK", "COVER", "NDAYS", "MAXNCE", "AVGNCE", "AVGDF", "BRENUMB", "BREAMOUNT" )
AS
SELECT 
 CASE 
 WHEN ST.DIVISCODE = 'E' THEN 'Equity'
 WHEN ST.DIVISCODE = 'L' THEN 'Idex'
 WHEN ST.DIVISCODE = 'W' THEN 'Agricultural'
 WHEN ST.DIVISCODE = 'O' THEN 'Fixed Income'
 END AS DIVISCODE, 
 CASE WHEN ST.DIVISCODE = 'O' THEN B.BNKRANK-1 ELSE B.BNKRANK END AS BNKRANK,
 CASE WHEN ST.DIVISCODE = 'C' THEN 1 ELSE 2 END AS COVER,
 CASE WHEN ST.DIVISCODE = 'O' THEN 5 ELSE 3 END AS NDAYS,
 MAX(ABS(CASE WHEN ((ST.DIVISCODE = 'O' AND B.BNKRANK IN (2,3)) OR (ST.DIVISCODE IN ('E','L') AND B.BNKRANK IN (1,2))) THEN NCECUM ELSE 0 END)) AS MAXNCE,
 ROUND(AVG(ABS(NCECUM)),2) AS AVGNCE,
 ROUND(AVG(ABS(DF)),2) AS AVGDF,
 SUM(CASE WHEN ((ST.DIVISCODE = 'O' AND B.BNKRANK IN (2,3)) OR (ST.DIVISCODE IN ('E','L') AND B.BNKRANK IN (1,2))) AND (ABS(NCECUM)>DF+SIG) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS BRENUMB,
 SUM(CASE WHEN ((ST.DIVISCODE = 'O' AND B.BNKRANK IN (2,3)) OR (ST.DIVISCODE IN ('E','L') AND B.BNKRANK IN (1,2))) AND (ABS(NCECUM)>DF+SIG) THEN ABS(NCECUM)-(DF+SIG) ELSE 0 END) AS BREAMOUNT
FROM PAMPITE.PMPVSTBNKS B
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST ON ST.STID = B.STID AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
WHERE ST.DIVISCODE IN ('E','L','O')
AND ST.LSTHISTDAT >= NOW() - 1 YEAR
AND B.SCENARIO IN ('I','D')
AND ((ST.DIVISCODE = 'O' AND B.BNKRANK IN (2,3)) OR (ST.DIVISCODE IN ('E','L') AND B.BNKRANK IN (1,2)))
GROUP BY ST.DIVISCODE,B.BNKRANK 
GO
RENAME TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVIOSCOST" TO SYSTEM NAME "PMPVI00003"
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVIRTCLM" ( "CLASSID", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "SENDDATE", "STATUS", "CRMARGIN", "CRCOVER", "CRNDAYSPER", "CRNV", "ANMARGIN", "ANCOVER", "ANNDAYSPER", "ANNV", "USERMARGIN", "ANDATE", "PROPCOVER", "PROPMARGIN", "APPROVAL", "RCCODE", "COMMENT", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE", "PROPOSE", "CRLOG", "ANLOG", "PROPLOG", "USERCOV", "CRFRSTHISD", "ANFRSTHISD", "ANLASTHISD", "CRLASTHISD", "SUSP", "CUSTOM", "CRNODEID", "ANNODEID", "DIVISCODE", "CLASSDESC", "CLDIVIS", "WORKMAR", "WORKFROMDT", "CHMAR", "CRNODES", "CRCURVES", "ANNODES", "ANCURVE", "CRMAXRATE", "CRMINRATE", "CRMINDUR", "CRMAXDUR", "ANMAXRATE", "ANMINRATE", "ANMINDUR", "ANMAXDUR" )
AS
SELECT M.CLASSID, M.INIVDATE, M.ENDVDATE, M.SENDDATE, M.STATUS, M.CRMARGIN, M.CRCOVER, 
M.CRNDAYSPER, M.CRNV, M.ANMARGIN, M.ANCOVER, M.ANNDAYSPER, M.ANNV, M.USERMARGIN, M.ANDATE, 
M.PROPCOVER, M.PROPMARGIN, M.APPROVAL, M.RCCODE, M.COMMENT, M.UPDTYPE, M.UPDUSR, M.UPDDATE, 
M.PROPOSE, M.CRLOG, M.ANLOG, M.PROPLOG, M.USERCOV, M.CRFRSTHISD, M.ANFRSTHISD, M.ANLASTHISD, 
M.CRLASTHISD, M.SUSP, M.CUSTOM, M.CRNODEID, M.ANNODEID, M.DIVISCODE, C.CLASSDESC, C.DIVISCODE AS CLDIVIS, 
H.MARGIN AS WORKMAR, H.INIVDATE AS WORKFROMDT, (M.PROPMARGIN-H.MARGIN)/M.PROPMARGIN AS CHMAR,
M.CRNODES,M.CRCURVES,M.ANNODES,M.ANCURVE,
M.CRMAXRATE,M.CRMINRATE,M.CRMINDUR,M.CRMAXDUR,
M.ANMAXRATE,M.ANMINRATE,M.ANMINDUR,M.ANMAXDUR
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTIRTCLM M 
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTIRTCLS C ON M.CLASSID=C.CLASSID 
LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTIRCLMH H ON M.CLASSID=H.CLASSID 
WHERE NOT EXISTS( SELECT Z.INIVDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTIRCLMH Z WHERE Z.INIVDATE>H.INIVDATE AND Z.CLASSID=H.CLASSID) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVLASTPR" ( "INSTRID", "PRICEDATE", "CLOSEPR", "STATUS", "UPDTYPE", "UPDDATE", "UPDUSR" )
AS
SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR T WHERE PRICEDATE>= ALL( SELECT PRICEDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR I WHERE I.INSTRID=T.INSTRID) 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVLASTPR" IS 'LAST ROW OF HISTORICAL PRICES PER INSTR.'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVLSTPRD" ( "INSTRID", "PRICEDATE", "PC", "STRIKE", "EXPIRY", "CODE", "STATUS", "CLOSEPR", "IMPVOLA", "UPDDATE", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR" )
AS
SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISDE T WHERE PRICEDATE>= ALL( SELECT PRICEDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISDE I WHERE I.INSTRID=T.INSTRID) 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVLSTPRD" IS 'LAST ROW OF DERIVATIVES HIST. PRICES PER INSTR.'
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVMAR" ( "INSTRID", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "SENDDATE", "STATUS", "CRMARGIN", "CRCOVER", "CRNDAYSPER" FOR "CURRN00001", "CRNV", "CRVARTYPE" FOR "CURRV00001", "ANMARGIN", "ANCOVER", "ANNDAYSPER", "ANNV", "ANVARTYPE", "USERMARGIN", "CRMINMAR", "ANMINMAR", "USERMINMAR", "ANDATE", "PROPCOVER", "PROPMARGIN", "PROPMINMAR", "APPROVAL", "RCCODE", "COMMENT", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE", "CLASSID", "CRNDMAR", "PROPOSE", "ANNDMAR", "CRLOG", "ANLOG", "PROPLOG", "USERCOV", "USERCH", "RLMARGIN", "CRFRSTHISD", "ANFRSTHISD", "ANLASTHISD", "CRLASTHISD", "SUSP", "CUSTOM", "DIVISCODE", "WORKMAR", "WORKMINMAR", "WORKFROMDT", "CHANMAR", "CHUSRMAR", "CHMAR", "CHMINMAR", "INSTRNAME", "CLASSCODE", "ISINCODE", "INDUSTRY", "SUPERSECT" )
AS
SELECT M.INSTRID, M.INIVDATE, M.ENDVDATE, M.SENDDATE, M.STATUS, M.CRMARGIN, M.CRCOVER, M.CRNDAYSPER, M.CRNV, M.CRVARTYPE, M.ANMARGIN, M.ANCOVER, M.ANNDAYSPER, M.ANNV, M.ANVARTYPE, M.USERMARGIN, M.CRMINMAR, M.ANMINMAR, M.USERMINMAR, M.ANDATE, M.PROPCOVER, M.PROPMARGIN, M.PROPMINMAR, M.APPROVAL, M.RCCODE, M.COMMENT, M.UPDTYPE, M.UPDUSR, M.UPDDATE, M.CLASSID, M.CRNDMAR, M.PROPOSE, M.ANNDMAR, M.CRLOG, M.ANLOG, M.PROPLOG, M.USERCOV, M.USERCH, M.RLMARGIN, M.CRFRSTHISD, M.ANFRSTHISD, M.ANLASTHISD, M.CRLASTHISD, M.SUSP, M.CUSTOM, M.DIVISCODE , H.MARGIN AS WORKMAR,H.MINMARGIN AS WORKMINMAR, H.INIVDATE AS WORKFROMDT, (M.ANMARGIN-H.MARGIN)/H.MARGIN AS CHANMAR, (M.USERMARGIN-H.MARGIN)/H.MARGIN AS CHUSRMAR, (M.PROPMARGIN-H.MARGIN)/M.PROPMARGIN AS CHMAR, (M.PROPMINMAR-H.MINMARGIN)/M.PROPMINMAR AS CHMINMAR, E.INSTRNAME, E.CLASSCODE, E.ISINCODE, E.INDUSTRY, E.SUPERSECT FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMAR M INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR E ON M.INSTRID=E.INSTRID LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS H ON M.INSTRID=H.INSTRID WHERE NOT EXISTS( SELECT Z.INIVDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS Z WHERE Z.INIVDATE>H.INIVDATE AND Z.INSTRID=H.INSTRID) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVMBTSIM" ( "BTID", "CLASSID", "CLASSDESC", "HCTDATE", "BTSIMHCT", "STATUS", "DIVISCODE", "MINRATE" FOR "HCL_M00001", "MAXRATE" FOR "HCL_M00002", "MINDUR" FOR "HCL_M00003", "MAXDUR" FOR "HCL_M00004", "SUPTH", "INFTH", "SIMUSRBRCH", "SIMWRKBRCH", "SIMADJBRCH", "SIMUSRCOV", "SIMUSRDAYS", "WRKADJBRCH", "WRKCOV", "WRKBRCH", "WRKHCT", "TOTWORKBREACH" FOR "TOTWO00001" )
AS
SELECT STAT.BTID, 
 HCL.CLASSID,
 HCL.CLASSDESC,
 HCL.HCTDATE,
 HCL.BTSIMHCT, 
 HCL.STATUS, 
 HCL.DIVISCODE,
 HCL.MINRATE,
 HCL.MAXRATE,
 HCL.MINDUR,
 HCL.MAXDUR,
 IFNULL(BRC.SUPTH,1000000) AS SUPTH, 
 IFNULL(BRC.INFTH,-1000000) AS INFTH, 
 IFNULL(BRC.USRBRCH,0) AS SIMUSRBRCH, 
 IFNULL(BRC.WRKBRCH,0) AS SIMWRKBRCH, 
 IFNULL(BRC.ADJBRCH,0) AS SIMADJBRCH, 
 IFNULL(BRC.USRCOV,1) AS SIMUSRCOV, 
 IFNULL(BRC.USRDAYS,0) AS SIMUSRDAYS,
 IFNULL(STAT.WRKADJBRCH,0) AS WRKADJBRCH, 
 IFNULL(STAT.WRKCOV,1) AS WRKCOV, 
 IFNULL(STAT.WRKBRCH,0) AS WRKBRCH, 
 STAT.WRKHCT,
 (IFNULL(STAT.WRKADJBRCH,0)+IFNULL(STAT.WRKBRCH,0)) AS TOTWORKBREACH
 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTHCL HCL 
 LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMXBTST STAT ON HCL.CLASSID=STAT.CLASSID 
 LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMSMBRC BRC ON HCL.CLASSID = BRC.CLASSID AND BRC.COUNTER = 0 AND (HCL.BTSIMHCT>=BRC.INFTH AND HCL.BTSIMHCT < BRC.SUPTH)
 WHERE HCL.DIVISCODE='M' AND STAT.BTID=(SELECT MAX(BTID) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMSMBRC) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVMICHISTHC" ( "INSTRID", "INSTRNAME", "ISINCODE", "PRICEDATE", "HAIRCUT", "DURATION" )
AS
SELECT A.INSTRID, I.INSTRNAME, I.ISINCODE, A.PRICEDATE, A.HAIRCUT, A.DURATION 
 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR A 
 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST 
 ON ST.STID = A.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I 
 ON I.INSTRID=A.INSTRID 
 WHERE A.PRICEDATE = 
 (SELECT MIN(B.PRICEDATE) 
 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR B 
 WHERE A.INSTRID=B.INSTRID AND B.STID IN (SELECT STID FROM PAMPITE.PMPTST WHERE DIVISCODE = 'M' AND STATUS = 'T' )) 
 
 UNION 
 
 SELECT M.INSTRID, I.INSTRNAME, I.ISINCODE,
 (SELECT M2.PRICEDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR M2 
 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST ON ST.STID = M2.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
 WHERE M2.INSTRID = M.INSTRID AND M2.STID > M.STID 
 FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY) AS PRICEDATE, 
 (SELECT M2.HAIRCUT FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR M2 
 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST ON ST.STID = M2.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
 WHERE M2.INSTRID = M.INSTRID AND M2.STID > M.STID 
 FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY) AS HAIRCUT,
 (SELECT M2.DURATION FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR M2 
 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST ON ST.STID = M2.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
 WHERE M2.INSTRID = M.INSTRID AND M2.STID > M.STID 
 FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY) AS DURATION
 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR M 
 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST ON ST.STID = M.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I 
 ON I.INSTRID=M.INSTRID 
 WHERE M.HAIRCUT <> (SELECT M2.HAIRCUT FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR M2 
 INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST ON ST.STID = M2.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
 WHERE M2.INSTRID = M.INSTRID AND M2.STID > M.STID 
 FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY) 
GO
RENAME TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVMICHISTHC" TO SYSTEM NAME "PMPVM00002"
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVMICHISTHCA" ( "INSTRID", "INSTRNAME", "PRICEDATE", "HAIRCUT" )
AS
(SELECT A.INSTRID, I.INSTRNAME,A.PRICEDATE, A.HAIRCUT 
	 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR A 
	INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST 
	ON ST.STID = A.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
	INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I 
	ON I.INSTRID=A.INSTRID 
	 WHERE A.PRICEDATE = 
	(SELECT MIN(B.PRICEDATE) 
	FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR B 
	WHERE A.INSTRID=B.INSTRID AND B.STID IN (SELECT STID FROM PAMPITE.PMPTST WHERE DIVISCODE = 'M' AND STATUS = 'T' )) 
	 
	UNION 
	 
	SELECT M.INSTRID, I.INSTRNAME, 
	(SELECT M2.PRICEDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR M2 
	INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST ON ST.STID = M2.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
	WHERE M2.INSTRID = M.INSTRID AND M2.STID > M.STID 
	FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY) AS PRICEDATE, 
	(SELECT M2.HAIRCUT FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR M2 
	INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST ON ST.STID = M2.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
	WHERE M2.INSTRID = M.INSTRID AND M2.STID > M.STID 
	FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY) AS HAIRCUT 
	FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR M 
	INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST ON ST.STID = M.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
	INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I 
	ON I.INSTRID=M.INSTRID 
	WHERE M.HAIRCUT <> (SELECT M2.HAIRCUT FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMICPR M2 
	INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTST ST ON ST.STID = M2.STID AND ST.DIVISCODE = 'M' AND ST.STATUS = 'T' 
	WHERE M2.INSTRID = M.INSTRID AND M2.STID > M.STID 
	FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY) 
	 
	 ) 
GO
RENAME TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVMICHISTHCA" TO SYSTEM NAME "PMPVM00001"
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVMINMAR" ( "INSTRID", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "SENDDATE", "STATUS", "CRMINMARM", "ANMINMAR", "USRMINMAR", "ANDATE", "PROPMINMAR", "PROPOSE", "APPROVAL", "RCCODE", "COMMENT", "CRLOG", "ANLOG", "PROPLOG", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE", "CUSTOM", "WORKMINMAR", "WORKFROMDT", "CHANMMAR", "CHUSRMMAR", "CHMINMAR" )
AS
SELECT M.*,H.MINMARGIN AS WORKMINMAR, H.INIVDATE AS WORKFROMDT, (M.ANMINMAR-H.MINMARGIN)/H.MINMARGIN AS CHANMMAR, (M.USRMINMAR-H.MINMARGIN)/H.MINMARGIN AS CHUSRMMAR, (M.PROPMINMAR-H.MINMARGIN)/H.MINMARGIN AS CHMINMAR FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMINMAR M LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS H ON M.INSTRID=H.INSTRID WHERE NOT EXISTS( SELECT Z.INIVDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS Z WHERE Z.INIVDATE>H.INIVDATE AND Z.INSTRID=H.INSTRID) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVMXBTGR" ( "BTID", "GROUPID", "GRPDESC", "WRKBRCH", "WRKADJBRCH", "ONDATEBRCH", "ONDADJBRCH", "NVARS", "WRKCOV", "ONDATECOV" )
AS
SELECT BTID,
	GROUPID,
	GRPDESC,
	SUM(WRKBRCH)AS WRKBRCH,
	SUM(WRKADJBRCH) AS WRKADJBRCH,
	SUM(ONDATEBRCH) AS ONDATEBRCH,
	SUM(ONDADJBRCH) AS ONDADJBRCH,
	SUM(NVARS) AS NVARS,
	CASE WHEN SUM(NVARS)=0 THEN 1 ELSE ROUND((DECIMAL((SUM(NVARS)-(SUM(WRKBRCH)+SUM(WRKADJBRCH))))/SUM(NVARS)),8) END AS WRKCOV,
	CASE WHEN SUM(NVARS)=0 THEN 1 ELSE ROUND((DECIMAL((SUM(NVARS)-(SUM(ONDATEBRCH)+SUM(ONDADJBRCH))))/SUM(NVARS)),8) END AS ONDATECOV
	FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMXBTST
	WHERE GROUPID>0
	GROUP BY BTID,GROUPID,GRPDESC 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVNOCAL" ( "PRICEDATE", "DIVISCODE", "MARKETCODE" )
AS
SELECT DISTINCT(PRICEDATE), I.DIVISCODE,'MTS' AS MARKETCODE 
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR H
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I ON H.INSTRID = I.INSTRID AND I.DIVISCODE IN ('B','H')
WHERE H.PRICEDATE NOT IN (SELECT DATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCALEND WHERE MARKETCODE = 'MTS') 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVRVAR" ( "INSTRID", "NV", "NDAYSPER", "VARTYPE", "STATUS", "MODE", "ND10", "NV10", "ND9", "NV9", "ND8", "NV8", "ND7", "NV7", "ND6", "NV6", "ND5", "NV5", "ND4", "NV4", "ND3", "NV3", "ND2", "NV2", "ND1", "NV1", "D1", "V1", "D2", "V2", "D3", "V3", "D4", "V4", "D5", "V5", "D6", "V6", "D7", "V7", "D8", "V8", "D9", "V9", "D10", "V10" )
AS
SELECT "PMPTRVAR"."INSTRID", "PMPTRVAR"."NV", "PMPTRVAR"."NDAYSPER", "PMPTRVAR"."VARTYPE", "PMPTRVAR"."STATUS", "PMPTRVAR"."MODE", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -10 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND10", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -10 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV10", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -9 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND9", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -9 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV9", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -8 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND8", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -8 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV8", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -7 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND7", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -7 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV7", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -6 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND6", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -6 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV6", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -5 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND5", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -5 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV5", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -4 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND4", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -4 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV4", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -3 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND3", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -3 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV3", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -2 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND2", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -2 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV2", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -1 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND1", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN -1 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV1", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 1 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D1", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 1 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V1", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 2 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D2", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 2 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V2", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 3 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D3", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 3 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V3", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 4 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D4", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 4 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V4", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 5 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D5", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 5 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V5", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 6 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D6", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 6 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V6", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 7 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D7", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 7 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V7", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 8 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D8", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 8 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V8", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 9 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D9", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 9 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V9", MAX(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 10 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D10", SUM(CASE "PMPTRVAR"."RANK" WHEN 10 THEN "PMPTRVAR"."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V10" FROM PAMPITE.PMPTRVAR "PMPTRVAR" GROUP BY "PMPTRVAR"."INSTRID", "PMPTRVAR"."NV", "PMPTRVAR"."NDAYSPER", "PMPTRVAR"."VARTYPE", "PMPTRVAR"."STATUS", "PMPTRVAR"."MODE" 
GO

CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVSETCMP" ( "SETID", "INSTRID", "INSTRNAME", "LISTNAME", "CLASSCODE", "RICCODE", "ISINCODE", "BLOOMBCODE", "DIVISCODE", "MARKETCODE", "SGMCODE", "INSTRTYPE", "INSTRSTYPE", "CURRENCY", "DISABREAS", "ADDRSTREET", "ADDRCITY", "ADDRDIST", "ADDRPC", "ADDRSTATE", "ADDRCOUNT", "HISTPRID", "HISTVOLAID", "DELISTREAS", "DELISTDATE", "INDUSTRY", "COMPOS", "ISSUER", "DIVTYPE", "ADDRWEB", "BMKNAME", "BMKRIC", "BMKRETURN", "BMKSTYLE", "BMKAREA", "BMKDESCR", "BMKCOMP", "BMKSPEC", "BMKCURR", "BMKNINSTR", "STATUS", "FORMAT", "SHORTTFUT", "LONGTOPT", "FUTEXPNUMB", "MULT", "SHORTOPADJ", "DELDAYS", "IRNODE", "IRNODEDESC", "REPORTING", "NOTE", "UPDTYPE", "UPDDATE", "UPDUSR", "MKTLSTDATE", "CCPLSTDATE", "SUPERSECT", "OPTEXPNUMB", "STRATYPE", "UNDINSTRID", "DEFHISTSER", "MARGINTH", "DERHIST", "MINMARTYPE", "COMPARABLE", "RCCODE", "SETTLETYPE", "BNDCLASSID", "DURATION", "MMTABLE", "DEFMARG" )
AS
SELECT 0 AS SETID,I1.INSTRID, I1.INSTRNAME, I1.LISTNAME, I1.CLASSCODE, I1.RICCODE, I1.ISINCODE, I1.BLOOMBCODE, I1.DIVISCODE, I1.MARKETCODE, I1.SGMCODE, I1.INSTRTYPE, I1.INSTRSTYPE, I1.CURRENCY, I1.DISABREAS, I1.ADDRSTREET, I1.ADDRCITY, I1.ADDRDIST, I1.ADDRPC, I1.ADDRSTATE, I1.ADDRCOUNT, I1.HISTPRID, I1.HISTVOLAID, I1.DELISTREAS, I1.DELISTDATE, I1.INDUSTRY, I1.COMPOS, I1.ISSUER, I1.DIVTYPE, I1.ADDRWEB, I1.BMKNAME, I1.BMKRIC, I1.BMKRETURN, I1.BMKSTYLE, I1.BMKAREA, I1.BMKDESCR, I1.BMKCOMP, I1.BMKSPEC, I1.BMKCURR, I1.BMKNINSTR, I1.STATUS, I1.FORMAT, I1.SHORTTFUT, I1.LONGTOPT, I1.FUTEXPNUMB, I1.MULT, I1.SHORTOPADJ, I1.DELDAYS, I1.IRNODE, I1.IRNODEDESC, I1.REPORTING, I1.NOTE, I1.UPDTYPE, I1.UPDDATE, I1.UPDUSR, I1.MKTLSTDATE, I1.CCPLSTDATE, I1.SUPERSECT, I1.OPTEXPNUMB, I1.STRATYPE, I1.UNDINSTRID, I1.DEFHISTSER, I1.MARGINTH, I1.DERHIST, I1.MINMARTYPE, I1.COMPARABLE, I1.RCCODE, I1.SETTLETYPE, I1.BNDCLASSID, I1.DURATION, I1.MMTABLE, I1.DEFMARG FROM PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I1 UNION SELECT C.SETID,I.INSTRID, I.INSTRNAME, I.LISTNAME, I.CLASSCODE, I.RICCODE, I.ISINCODE, I.BLOOMBCODE, I.DIVISCODE, I.MARKETCODE, I.SGMCODE, I.INSTRTYPE, I.INSTRSTYPE, I.CURRENCY, I.DISABREAS, I.ADDRSTREET, I.ADDRCITY, I.ADDRDIST, I.ADDRPC, I.ADDRSTATE, I.ADDRCOUNT, I.HISTPRID, I.HISTVOLAID, I.DELISTREAS, I.DELISTDATE, I.INDUSTRY, I.COMPOS, I.ISSUER, I.DIVTYPE, I.ADDRWEB, I.BMKNAME, I.BMKRIC, I.BMKRETURN, I.BMKSTYLE, I.BMKAREA, I.BMKDESCR, I.BMKCOMP, I.BMKSPEC, I.BMKCURR, I.BMKNINSTR, I.STATUS, I.FORMAT, I.SHORTTFUT, I.LONGTOPT, I.FUTEXPNUMB, I.MULT, I.SHORTOPADJ, I.DELDAYS, I.IRNODE, I.IRNODEDESC, I.REPORTING, I.NOTE, I.UPDTYPE, I.UPDDATE, I.UPDUSR, I.MKTLSTDATE, I.CCPLSTDATE, I.SUPERSECT, I.OPTEXPNUMB, I.STRATYPE, I.UNDINSTRID, I.DEFHISTSER, I.MARGINTH, I.DERHIST, I.MINMARTYPE, I.COMPARABLE, I.RCCODE, I.SETTLETYPE, I.BNDCLASSID, I.DURATION, I.MMTABLE, I.DEFMARG FROM PAMPITE.PMPTSETCMP C INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I ON I.INSTRID=C.INSTRID 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVSMCONF" ( "INSTRID", "NDAYSPER", "NDAYSDESC", "NV", "STATUS", "UNCEV", "CONFIDENCE", "COVPERC", "UPDUSR", "UPDTYPE", "UPDDATE" )
AS
SELECT PMPTSMCONF.INSTRID, PMPTSMCONF.NDAYSPER,PMPTPER.NDAYSDESC, PMPTSMCONF.NV,PMPTSMCONF.STATUS,PMPTSMCONF.UNCEV, PMPTSMCONF.CONFIDENCE,PMPTSMCONF.COVPERC, PMPTSMCONF.UPDUSR, PMPTSMCONF.UPDTYPE, PMPTSMCONF.UPDDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTSMCONF PMPTSMCONF INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTPER PMPTPER ON PMPTPER.NDAYSPER=PMPTSMCONF.NDAYSPER WHERE UNCEVSEL=UNCEV 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVSMRVAR" ( "INSTRID", "NV", "NDAYSPER", "VARTYPE", "MODE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE", "UPDTYPE", "ND10", "NV10", "ND9", "NV9", "ND8", "NV8", "ND7", "NV7", "ND6", "NV6", "ND5", "NV5", "ND4", "NV4", "ND3", "NV3", "ND2", "NV2", "ND1", "NV1", "D1", "V1", "D2", "V2", "D3", "V3", "D4", "V4", "D5", "V5", "D6", "V6", "D7", "V7", "D8", "V8", "D9", "V9", "D10", "V10" )
AS
SELECT T."INSTRID", T."NV", T."NDAYSPER", T."VARTYPE", T."MODE", MAX(T.UPDUSR) AS UPDUSR, MAX(T.UPDDATE) AS UPDDATE, MAX(T.UPDTYPE) AS UPDTYPE, MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -10 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND10", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -10 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV10", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -9 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND9", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -9 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV9", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -8 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND8", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -8 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV8", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -7 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND7", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -7 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV7", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -6 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND6", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -6 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV6", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -5 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND5", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -5 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV5", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -4 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND4", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -4 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV4", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -3 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND3", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -3 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV3", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -2 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND2", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -2 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV2", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -1 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "ND1", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN -1 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "NV1", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 1 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D1", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 1 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V1", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 2 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D2", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 2 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V2", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 3 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D3", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 3 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V3", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 4 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D4", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 4 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V4", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 5 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D5", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 5 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V5", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 6 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D6", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 6 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V6", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 7 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D7", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 7 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V7", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 8 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D8", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 8 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V8", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 9 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D9", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 9 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V9", MAX(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 10 THEN T."PRICEDATE" ELSE '1890-03-02-08.30.00.100000' END) AS "D10", SUM(CASE T."RANK" WHEN 10 THEN T."VARIAT" ELSE 0 END) AS "V10" FROM PAMPITE.PMPTSMRVAR T GROUP BY T."INSTRID", T."NV", T."NDAYSPER", T."VARTYPE", T."MODE"
