CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVSTBNKI" ( "BNKRANK", "SCENARIO", "STID", "OLDRANK", "MBRBNKGRID", "GMBBNKGRID", "MBRBNKGRNM", "GMBBNKGRNM", "DFINIVDATE", "NCECUM", "NCERCUM", "NCESUM", "NCE", "DF", "LASTINDF", "TOTEXPOSED", "TOTMEMBERS" )
AS
SELECT
(CASE WHEN M1.BNKRANK<M.BNKRANK THEN M.BNKRANK-1 ELSE M.BNKRANK END) AS BNKRANK, 
M.SCENARIO, M.STID, M.BNKRANK AS OLDRANK, M.MBRBNKGRID, M.GMBBNKGRID, M.MBRBNKGRNM, M.GMBBNKGRNM, 
M.DFINIVDATE, M.NCECUM,M.NCERCUM, M.NCESUM,M.NCE,M.DF,M.LASTINDF,M.TOTEXPOSED,M.TOTBNKGR AS TOTMEMBERS 
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTSTBNKS M 
LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTSTBNKS M1 
ON M.STID=M1.STID AND
M1.SCENARIO=M.SCENARIO AND
M1.MBRBNKGRID = 21323 
WHERE M.MBRBNKGRID != 21323 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVSTBNKS" ( "BNKRANK", "SCENARIO", "STID", "OLDRANK", "MBRBNKGRID", "GMBBNKGRID", "MBRBNKGRNM", "GMBBNKGRNM", "DFINIVDATE", "NCECUM", "NCERCUM", "NCESUM", "NCE", "DF", "SIG", "LASTINDF", "TOTEXPOSED", "TOTMEMBERS" )
AS
(SELECT 
					(CASE WHEN M1.BNKRANK>M.BNKRANK THEN M.BNKRANK+1 WHEN M1.BNKRANK=M.BNKRANK THEN 1 ELSE M.BNKRANK END) AS BNKRANK, 
					M.SCENARIO, M.STID, M.BNKRANK AS OLDRANK, M.MBRBNKGRID, M.GMBBNKGRID, M.MBRBNKGRNM, M.GMBBNKGRNM, M.DFINIVDATE, 
					M.NCECUM,M.NCERCUM, M.NCESUM,M.NCE, 
					M.DF, M.SIG, M.LASTINDF,M.TOTEXPOSED,M.TOTBNKGR AS TOTMEMBERS 
					 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTSTBNKS M 
					 LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTSTBNKS M1 ON M.STID=M1.STID AND M1.SCENARIO=M.SCENARIO AND M1.MBRBNKGRID = 21323) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVSTMBRS" ( "MBRRANK", "SCENARIO", "STID", "MBRID", "GMBRID", "MBRDESC", "GMBRDESC", "HISTUPDDAY", "LOG", "NVVEC", "NDAYSPER", "MMTMARGIN", "ORDMARGIN", "DFQUOTAD", "HNRMMAR", "CNRMMAR", "HSTRMAR", "CSTRMAR", "NCE", "NCECUM", "NCERCUM", "NCESUM", "DF", "SIG", "MIA", "DFINIVDATE", "LASTINDF", "TOTEXPOSED", "TOTMEMBERS", "UPDDATE", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR" )
AS
SELECT (CASE WHEN M1.MBRRANK>M.MBRRANK AND M.SCENARIO='D' THEN M.MBRRANK+1 WHEN M1.MBRRANK=M.MBRRANK AND M.SCENARIO='D' THEN 1 ELSE M.MBRRANK END) AS MBRRANK, M.SCENARIO, M.STID, M.MBRID, M.GMBRID, M.MBRDESC, M.GMBRDESC, M.HISTUPDDAY, M."LOG", M.NVVEC, M.NDAYSPER, M.MMTMARGIN, M.ORDMARGIN,M.DFQUOTAD, M.HNRMMAR, M.CNRMMAR, M.HSTRMAR, M.CSTRMAR, M.NCE, M.NCECUM, M.NCERCUM, M.NCESUM, M.DF, M.SIG, M.MIA, M.DFINIVDATE, M.LASTINDF, M.TOTEXPOSED, M.TOTMEMBERS, M.UPDDATE, M.UPDTYPE, M.UPDUSR 
		FROM PAMPITE.PMPTSTMBRS M 
		LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTSTMBRS M1 ON M.STID=M1.STID AND M1.SCENARIO=M.SCENARIO AND M1.MBRID = 1323 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVSTRA" ( "INSTRID", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "SENDDATE", "STATUS", "CRSTRAM", "ANSTRA", "USRSTRA", "ANDATE", "PROPSTRA", "CRMUL", "ANMUL", "USRMUL", "CRSPREAD", "ANSPREAD", "USRSPREAD", "PROPOSE", "APPROVAL", "RCCODE", "COMMENT", "CRLOG", "ANLOG", "PROPLOG", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "UPDDATE", "ANNV", "CRNV", "ANNDAYSPER", "CRNDAYSPER", "ANPRGEXP1", "CRPRGEXP1", "ANPRGEXP2", "CRPRGEXP2", "ANSTRTYPE", "CRSTRTYPE", "CUSTOM", "WORKSTRA", "WORKFROMDT", "CHANSTRA", "CHUSRSTRA", "CHSTRA" )
AS
SELECT S.*,H.STRADDLE AS WORKSTRA, H.INIVDATE AS WORKFROMDT, (S.ANSTRA-H.STRADDLE)/H.STRADDLE AS CHANSTRA, (S.USRSTRA-H.STRADDLE)/H.STRADDLE AS CHUSRSTRA , (S.PROPSTRA-H.STRADDLE)/H.STRADDLE AS CHSTRA FROM PAMPITE.PMPTSTRA S LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS H ON S.INSTRID=H.INSTRID WHERE NOT EXISTS( SELECT Z.INIVDATE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS Z WHERE Z.INIVDATE>H.INIVDATE AND Z.INSTRID=H.INSTRID) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVSTSTAD" ( "INSTRID", "CLASSCODE", "INSTRNAME", "DIVISCODE", "INSTRTYPE", "INSTRSTYPE", "BNDCLASSID", "SCENARIO", "STID", "EXTRN", "EXTRNV", "IRCURVEID", "EXTRS", "EXTRRES", "MARRES", "STDEVRES", "SCRES", "HISTUPDDAY", "LOG", "CHOOSENFUN", "MARDER", "MARLOG", "MARPROP", "MARUSED", "NVVEC", "NDAYSPER", "STDEV", "STATUS", "CLOSEPR", "CLOSEPRST", "UPDDATE", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "IDXNVVEC", "IDXEXTRN", "IDXEXTRNV", "IDXEXTRS", "IDXEXTRRES", "IDXCUSTRES" )
AS
SELECT I.INSTRID, I.CLASSCODE, I.INSTRNAME, I.DIVISCODE, I.INSTRTYPE, I.INSTRSTYPE, I.BNDCLASSID, S.SCENARIO, S.STID, S.EXTRN, S.EXTRNV, S.IRCURVEID, S.EXTRS, S.EXTRRES, S.MARRES, 
	S.STDEVRES, S.SCRES, S.HISTUPDDAY, S.LOG, S.CHOOSENFUN, S.MARDER, S.MARLOG, S.MARPROP, S.MARUSED, S.NVVEC, S.NDAYSPER, S.STDEV, S.STATUS, 
	HI.CLOSEPR, HI.CLOSEPRST, S.UPDDATE, S.UPDTYPE, S.UPDUSR, S.IDXNVVEC, S.IDXEXTRN, S.IDXEXTRNV, S.IDXEXTRS, S.IDXEXTRRES, S.IDXCUSTRES 
	FROM PAMPUAT.PMPTSTSTAT S 
	INNER JOIN PAMPUAT.PMPTINSTR I ON I.INSTRID=S.INSTRID 
	LEFT JOIN PAMPUAT.PMPTSTHISD HI ON S.INSTRID=HI.INSTRID AND S.STID=HI.STID AND HI.SCENARIO=S.SCENARIO 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVSTSTAT" ( "INSTRID", "CLASSCODE", "INSTRNAME", "DIVISCODE", "INSTRTYPE", "INSTRSTYPE", "BNDCLASSID", "SCENARIO", "STID", "EXTRN", "EXTRNV", "IRCURVEID", "EXTRS", "EXTRRES", "MARRES", "STDEVRES", "SCRES", "HISTUPDDAY", "LOG", "CHOOSENFUN", "MARDER", "MARLOG", "MARPROP", "MARUSED", "NVVEC", "NDAYSPER", "STDEV", "STATUS", "CLOSEPR", "CLOSEPRST", "UPDDATE", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "IDXNVVEC", "IDXEXTRN", "IDXEXTRNV", "IDXEXTRS", "IDXEXTRRES", "IDXCUSTRES", "LSTVARVAL", "APPSCEN" )
AS
SELECT I.INSTRID, I.CLASSCODE, I.INSTRNAME, I.DIVISCODE, I.INSTRTYPE, I.INSTRSTYPE, I.BNDCLASSID, S.SCENARIO, S.STID, S.EXTRN, S.EXTRNV, S.IRCURVEID, 
S.EXTRS, S.EXTRRES, S.MARRES, S.STDEVRES, S.SCRES, S.HISTUPDDAY, S.LOG, S.CHOOSENFUN, S.MARDER, S.MARLOG, S.MARPROP, S.MARUSED, S.NVVEC, S.NDAYSPER, 
S.STDEV, S.STATUS, HI.CLOSEPR, HI.CLOSEPRST, S.UPDDATE, S.UPDTYPE, S.UPDUSR, S.IDXNVVEC, S.IDXEXTRN, S.IDXEXTRNV, S.IDXEXTRS, S.IDXEXTRRES, S.IDXCUSTRES,
S.LSTVARVAL, S.APPSCEN 
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTSTSTAT S 
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I ON I.INSTRID=S.INSTRID 
LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTSTHISP HI ON S.INSTRID=HI.INSTRID AND S.STID=HI.STID AND HI.SCENARIO=S.SCENARIO 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVTERTRA" ( "CLASSID1", "CLASSDSC1", "CLASSID2", "CLASSDSC2", "DIVIS1", "DIVIS2", "INIVDATE", "ENDVDATE", "SENDDATE", "STATUS", "ANOFF", "ANINSTRID1", "ANINSTRID2", "ANNDAYSPER", "ANNV", "USEROFF", "ANDATE", "PROPOFF", "PROPOSE", "ANFRSTHISD", "ANLASTHISD", "WORKOFF", "WORKSTATUS", "PRIORITY" )
AS
( ( SELECT T1.CLASSID AS CLASSID1, I1.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDSC1, T1.CLASSID AS CLASSID2 , I1.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDSC2, I1.DIVISCODE AS DIVIS1, I1.DIVISCODE AS DIVIS2, T1.INIVDATE, T1.ENDVDATE, T1.SENDDATE, T1.STATUS, T1.ANOFF,T1.ANINSTRID1, T1.ANINSTRID2, T1.ANNDAYSPER, T1.ANNV, T1.USEROFF, T1.ANDATE, T1.PROPOFF, T1.PROPOSE, T1.ANFRSTHISD, T1.ANLASTHISD, TH.OFF AS WORKOFF, TH.STATUS AS WORKSTATUS, 
	ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY T1.CLASSID ASC) PRIORITY FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTRA T1
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS I1 ON T1.CLASSID=I1.CLASSID
LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLTRAH TH ON T1.CLASSID=TH.CLASSID 
WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTRAH TH1 WHERE T1.CLASSID=TH1.CLASSID AND TH.INIVDATE<TH1.INIVDATE) 

AND T1.STATUS='E'
AND ( (TH.STATUS='D' AND T1.PROPOSE='A') OR (TH.STATUS='E' AND T1.PROPOSE='L') OR T1.PROPOSE='C')

ORDER BY T1.CLASSID )

UNION

( SELECT T1.CLASSID1, I1.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDSC1, T1.CLASSID2, I2.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDSC2, I1.DIVISCODE AS DIVIS1, I2.DIVISCODE AS DIVIS2, T1.INIVDATE, T1.ENDVDATE, T1.SENDDATE, T1.STATUS, T1.ANOFF, T1.ANINSTRID1, T1.ANINSTRID2, T1.ANNDAYSPER, T1.ANNV, T1.USEROFF, T1.ANDATE, T1.PROPOFF, T1.PROPOSE, T1.ANFRSTHISD, T1.ANLASTHISD, TH.OFF AS WORKOFF, TH.STATUS AS WORKSTATUS, 
(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY T1.CLASSID1,T1.CLASSID2 ASC))+ (SELECT COUNT(*)
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTRA
WHERE STATUS='E') AS PRIORITY
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTER T1
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS I1 ON T1.CLASSID1=I1.CLASSID
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS I2 ON T1.CLASSID2=I2.CLASSID
LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLTERH TH ON T1.CLASSID1=TH.CLASSID1 AND T1.CLASSID2=TH.CLASSID2
WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTERH TH1 WHERE T1.CLASSID1=TH1.CLASSID1 AND T1.CLASSID2=TH1.CLASSID2 AND TH.INIVDATE<TH1.INIVDATE) 

AND T1.STATUS='E' 
AND ( (TH.STATUS='D' AND T1.PROPOSE='A') OR (TH.STATUS='E' AND T1.PROPOSE='L') OR T1.PROPOSE='C')

ORDER BY T1.CLASSID1,T1.CLASSID2 )

UNION

( SELECT T1.CLASSID2 AS CLASSID1, I2.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDSC1, T1.CLASSID1 AS CLASSID2, I1.CLASSDESC AS CLASSDSC2, I1.DIVISCODE AS DIVIS1, I2.DIVISCODE AS DIVIS2, T1.INIVDATE, T1.ENDVDATE, T1.SENDDATE, T1.STATUS, T1.ANOFF, T1.ANINSTRID1, T1.ANINSTRID2,T1.ANNDAYSPER, T1.ANNV, T1.USEROFF, T1.ANDATE, T1.PROPOFF, T1.PROPOSE, T1.ANFRSTHISD, T1.ANLASTHISD, TH.OFF AS WORKOFF, TH.STATUS AS WORKSTATUS, 
(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY T1.CLASSID1,T1.CLASSID2 ASC))+ (SELECT COUNT(*)
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTRA
WHERE STATUS='E') AS PRIORITY
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTER T1
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS I1 ON T1.CLASSID1=I1.CLASSID
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLASS I2 ON T1.CLASSID2=I2.CLASSID
LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTCLTERH TH ON T1.CLASSID1=TH.CLASSID1 AND T1.CLASSID2=TH.CLASSID2
WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT * 	FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLTERH TH1
WHERE T1.CLASSID1=TH1.CLASSID1 AND T1.CLASSID2=TH1.CLASSID2 AND TH.INIVDATE<TH1.INIVDATE)

AND T1.STATUS='E'
AND ( (TH.STATUS='D' AND T1.PROPOSE='A') OR (TH.STATUS='E' AND T1.PROPOSE='L') OR T1.PROPOSE='C')

ORDER BY T1.CLASSID1,T1.CLASSID2 )) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVVAR" ( "INSTRID", "NV", "PRICEDATE", "VARTYPE", "VARIAT", "MARGIN", "CLMARGIN", "NEGMARGIN", "CURRMARGIN" )
AS
SELECT I.INSTRID, NV, PRICEDATE, VARTYPE, VARIAT,
 (
 SELECT H.MARGIN
 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTMARHIS H
 WHERE H.INIVDATE<=V.PRICEDATE
	AND V.INSTRID=H.INSTRID
	ORDER BY H.INIVDATE DESC
	FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY
	) AS MARGIN,
 (
 SELECT H.MARGIN
 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLMARH H
 WHERE H.INIVDATE<=V.PRICEDATE
 AND I.BNDCLASSID=H.CLASSID
 ORDER BY H.INIVDATE DESC
 FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY
 ) AS CLMARGIN,
 (
 SELECT -H.MARGIN
 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLMARH H
 WHERE H.INIVDATE<=V.PRICEDATE
 AND I.BNDCLASSID=H.CLASSID
 ORDER BY H.INIVDATE DESC
 FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY
 ) AS NEGMARGIN,
 (
 SELECT H.MARGIN
 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTCLMARH H
 WHERE I.BNDCLASSID=H.CLASSID
 ORDER BY H.INIVDATE DESC
 FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY
 ) AS CURRMARGIN
 
FROM PAMPITE.PMPTVAR V
INNER JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I 
ON I.INSTRID=V.INSTRID 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVVOLA" ( "INSTRID", "UNDINSTRID", "PRICEDATE", "PC", "STRIKE", "EXPIRY", "CODE", "STATUS", "CLOSEPR", "IMPVOLA", "UPDDATE", "UPDTYPE", "UPDUSR", "PRGEXP" )
AS
SELECT D.INSTRID, I.INSTRID AS UNDINSTRID, D.PRICEDATE, D.PC, D.STRIKE, D.EXPIRY, D.CODE, D.STATUS, D.CLOSEPR, D.IMPVOLA, D.UPDDATE, D.UPDTYPE, D.UPDUSR, (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT(EXPIRY)) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISDE D1 WHERE D.INSTRID=D1.INSTRID AND D.PRICEDATE=D1.PRICEDATE AND D.PC=D1.PC AND D.STRIKE=D1.STRIKE AND D1.EXPIRY<=D.EXPIRY ) AS PRGEXP FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISDE D, PAMPITE.PMPTINSTR I WHERE I.HISTVOLAID=D.INSTRID 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVXBTSIM" ( "BTID", "CLASSID", "CLASSDESC", "HCTDATE", "BTSIMHCT", "STATUS", "DIVISCODE", "MINRATE", "MAXRATE", "MINDUR", "MAXDUR", "SUPTH", "INFTH", "SIMUSRBRCH", "SIMWRKBRCH", "SIMADJBRCH", "SIMUSRCOV", "SIMUSRDAYS", "WRKADJBRCH", "WRKCOV", "WRKBRCH", "WRKHCT", "TOTWORKBREACH" FOR "TOTWO00001" )
AS
SELECT STAT.BTID, 
 HCL.CLASSID,
 HCL.CLASSDESC,
 HCL.HCTDATE,
 HCL.BTSIMHCT, 
 HCL.STATUS, 
 HCL.DIVISCODE,
 HCL.MINRATE,
 HCL.MAXRATE,
 HCL.MINDUR,
 HCL.MAXDUR,
 IFNULL(BRC.SUPTH,1000000) AS SUPTH, 
 IFNULL(BRC.INFTH,-1000000) AS INFTH, 
 IFNULL(BRC.USRBRCH,0) AS SIMUSRBRCH, 
 IFNULL(BRC.WRKBRCH,0) AS SIMWRKBRCH, 
 IFNULL(BRC.ADJBRCH,0) AS SIMADJBRCH, 
 IFNULL(BRC.USRCOV,1) AS SIMUSRCOV, 
 IFNULL(BRC.USRDAYS,0) AS SIMUSRDAYS,
 IFNULL(STAT.WRKADJBRCH,0) AS WRKADJBRCH, 
 IFNULL(STAT.WRKCOV,1) AS WRKCOV, 
 IFNULL(STAT.WRKBRCH,0) AS WRKBRCH, 
 STAT.WRKHCT,
 (IFNULL(STAT.WRKADJBRCH,0)+IFNULL(STAT.WRKBRCH,0)) AS TOTWORKBREACH
 FROM PAMPITE.PMPTBTHCL HCL 
 LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTMXBTST STAT ON HCL.CLASSID=STAT.CLASSID 
 LEFT JOIN PAMPITE.PMPTXSMBRC BRC ON HCL.CLASSID = BRC.CLASSID AND BRC.COUNTER = 0 AND (HCL.BTSIMHCT>=BRC.INFTH AND HCL.BTSIMHCT < BRC.SUPTH)
 WHERE HCL.DIVISCODE='S' AND STAT.BTID=(SELECT MAX(BTID) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTXSMBRC) 
GO
CREATE VIEW "PAMPITE"."PMPVZSCORE" ( "INSTRID", "PRICEDATE", "ZSCORE" )
AS
SELECT P.INSTRID,P.PRICEDATE, ( SELECT CAST(ABS(P.CLOSEPR-AVG(P1.CLOSEPR))/MAX(STDDEV(P1.CLOSEPR) , 0.01) AS FLOAT) FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR P1 WHERE ABS(DAYS(P.PRICEDATE)-DAYS(P1.PRICEDATE))<60 AND ABS(DAYS(P.PRICEDATE)-DAYS(P1.PRICEDATE))!=0 AND P1.INSTRID=P.INSTRID GROUP BY P1.INSTRID ) AS ZSCORE FROM PAMPITE.PMPTHISPR P 
GO
LABEL ON TABLE "PAMPITE"."PMPVZSCORE" IS 'ZSCORE STANDARDIZATION'
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSBTBRC" (IN IN_BTID INTEGER, IN IN_CLASSID INTEGER)
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC

DECLARE CNT INT DEFAULT 0 ;
DECLARE SQLSTATE CHAR ( 5 ) DEFAULT '00000' ;
DECLARE USER_DAYS INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
DECLARE BTCOV DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE NV_VAR INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE INSTR_ID INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PRDATE TIMESTAMP ;
		DECLARE BTCURSOR CURSOR FOR
			SELECT NV , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , IFNULL ( USRCOV , 0 ) FROM PMPTBTBRCH WHERE BTID = IN_BTID AND CLASSID = IN_CLASSID
			ORDER BY ABS ( USRMAR ) DESC ;

		--CONTA I RECORD PER POPOLARE USER_DATS 
SELECT COUNT ( BTID ) INTO USER_DAYS FROM PMPTBTBRCH WHERE BTID = IN_BTID AND CLASSID = IN_CLASSID ;
		
		OPEN BTCURSOR ;

		FETCH BTCURSOR INTO NV_VAR , INSTR_ID , PRDATE , BTCOV ;
		
		WHILE ( SQLSTATE = '00000' ) DO

			SET CNT = CNT + 1 ;
			SET BTCOV = 1.0 - ROUND ( ( CNT * 1.00 / USER_DAYS ) , 8 ) ;

			--UPDATE DEI CAMPI USRDAYS, USRCOV, USRBRCH
			UPDATE PMPTBTBRCH SET USRDAYS = USER_DAYS , USRCOV = BTCOV , USRBRCH = CNT , UPDDATE = NOW ( ) WHERE BTID = IN_BTID AND NV = NV_VAR AND CLASSID = IN_CLASSID AND INSTRID = INSTR_ID AND PRICEDATE = PRDATE ;
		
			FETCH BTCURSOR INTO NV_VAR , INSTR_ID , PRDATE , BTCOV ;
		END WHILE ;
		
		CLOSE BTCURSOR ;
	END 
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSERAST" (IN STRESS_ID INTEGER, IN STRESS_SCEN CHARACTER(1))
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC

DELETE FROM PMPTSTMBR WHERE STID = STRESS_ID AND SCENARIO = STRESS_SCEN ;
DELETE FROM PMPTSTMBRS WHERE STID = STRESS_ID AND SCENARIO = STRESS_SCEN ;
DELETE FROM PMPTSTBNKS WHERE STID = STRESS_ID AND SCENARIO = STRESS_SCEN ;
DELETE FROM PMPTSLOMBR WHERE STID = STRESS_ID AND SCENARIO = STRESS_SCEN ;
DELETE FROM PMPTSLOSTA WHERE STID = STRESS_ID AND SCENARIO = STRESS_SCEN ;
DELETE FROM PMPTBGSLST WHERE STID = STRESS_ID AND SCENARIO = STRESS_SCEN ;
DELETE FROM PMPTSTNCM WHERE STID = STRESS_ID AND SCENARIO = STRESS_SCEN ;
DELETE FROM PMPTSTDUCL WHERE STID = STRESS_ID AND SCENARIO = STRESS_SCEN ;
DELETE FROM PMPTESMCOL WHERE STID = STRESS_ID AND SCENARIO = STRESS_SCEN ;
END 
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSESMA" (IN IN_STID INTEGER, IN IN_SCENARIO CHARACTER(1))
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC DELETE FROM PAMPITE . ESMARPTS WHERE STID = IN_STID AND SCENARIO = IN_SCENARIO ; INSERT INTO PAMPITE . ESMARPTS ( STID , SCENARIO , MBRID , GENMBRID , SUBACCT , MBRNAME , GENMBRNAME , ACCTYPE , MTM , VAR_MAR , PRE_MAR , UPDDATE ) SELECT IN_STID , IN_SCENARIO , MTM . * , 0 , 0 , NOW ( ) FROM ( SELECT BK . MGMBRID AS MBRID , BK . MGGCMID AS GENMBRID , BK . MGSUBACT AS SUBACCOUNT , MBR01 . MFMNAM AS MBRNAME , MBR01B . MFMNAM AS GENMBRNAME , BK . MGACCT AS ACCTYPE , SUM ( BK . MGPRMTM ) AS MTM FROM I400DTAST . BKMS2200F BK INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01 ON BK . MGMBRID = MBR01 . MEXMEM INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01B ON BK . MGGCMID = MBR01B . MEXMEM WHERE MGSTLG NOT IN ( 'IDEX' , 'AGRX' ) GROUP BY BK . MGMBRID , BK . MGGCMID , MBR01 . MFMNAM , MBR01B . MFMNAM , BK . MGACCT , BK . MGSUBACT ORDER BY BK . MGMBRID , BK . MGACCT ) AS MTM ; MERGE INTO ESMARPTS A USING ( SELECT IN_STID AS STID , IN_SCENARIO AS SCENARIO , LMBR AS MBRID , LGCM AS GENMBRID , MBR01 . MFMNAM AS MBRNAME , MBR01B . MFMNAM AS GENMBRNAME , TRIM ( LSUBAC ) AS SUBACCT , LACCT AS ACCTYPE , SUM ( LSAMT ) AS VAR_MAR FROM I400DTAST . TLCSHS2 T INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01 ON T . LMBR = MBR01 . MEXMEM INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01B ON T . LGCM = MBR01B . MEXMEM WHERE LFO = 'F' AND LSTLGID NOT IN ( 'IDEX' , 'AGRX' ) GROUP BY LMBR , LGCM , LACCT , LSUBAC , MBR01 . MFMNAM , MBR01B . MFMNAM ORDER BY LMBR , LGCM , LACCT ) B ON ( A . STID = B . STID AND A . SCENARIO = B . SCENARIO AND A . MBRID = B . MBRID AND A . GENMBRID = B . GENMBRID AND A . SUBACCT = B . SUBACCT AND A . ACCTYPE = B . ACCTYPE ) WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET A . VAR_MAR = B . VAR_MAR , A . UPDDATE = NOW ( ) WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN INSERT ( STID , SCENARIO , MBRID , GENMBRID , SUBACCT , MBRNAME , GENMBRNAME , ACCTYPE , MTM , VAR_MAR ) VALUES ( B . STID , B . SCENARIO , B . MBRID , B . GENMBRID , B . SUBACCT , B . MBRNAME , B . GENMBRNAME , B . ACCTYPE , 0 , B . VAR_MAR ) ;
MERGE INTO ESMARPTS A USING ( SELECT IN_STID AS STID , IN_SCENARIO AS SCENARIO , LMBR AS MBRID , LGCM AS GENMBRID , MBR01 . MFMNAM AS MBRNAME , MBR01B . MFMNAM AS GENMBRNAME , TRIM ( LSUBAC ) AS SUBACCT , LACCT AS ACCTYPE , SUM ( LSAMT ) AS PRE_MAR FROM I400DTAST . TLCSHS2 T INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01 ON T . LMBR = MBR01 . MEXMEM INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01B ON T . LGCM = MBR01B . MEXMEM WHERE LFO = 'O' AND LSTLGID NOT IN ( 'IDEX' , 'AGRX' ) GROUP BY LMBR , LGCM , LACCT , LSUBAC , MBR01 . MFMNAM , MBR01B . MFMNAM ORDER BY LMBR , LGCM , LACCT ) B ON ( A . STID = B . STID AND A . SCENARIO = B . SCENARIO AND A . MBRID = B . MBRID AND A . GENMBRID = B . GENMBRID AND A . SUBACCT = B . SUBACCT AND A . ACCTYPE = B . ACCTYPE ) WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET A . PRE_MAR = B . PRE_MAR , A . UPDDATE = NOW ( ) WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN INSERT ( STID , SCENARIO , MBRID , GENMBRID , SUBACCT , MBRNAME , GENMBRNAME , ACCTYPE , MTM , PRE_MAR ) VALUES ( B . STID , B . SCENARIO , B . MBRID , B . GENMBRID , B . SUBACCT , B . MBRNAME , B . GENMBRNAME , B . ACCTYPE , 0 , B . PRE_MAR ) ;
END 
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSESMAB" (IN IN_STID INTEGER, IN IN_SCENARIO CHARACTER(1))
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC DELETE FROM PAMPITE . ESMARPTS WHERE STID = IN_STID AND SCENARIO = IN_SCENARIO ; INSERT INTO PAMPITE . ESMARPTS ( STID , SCENARIO , MBRID , GENMBRID , SUBACCT , MBRNAME , GENMBRNAME , ACCTYPE , MTM , VAR_MAR , UPDDATE ) SELECT IN_STID , IN_SCENARIO ,
CAST ( MS62 . MCDMBR AS INTEGER ) AS MBRID ,
CAST ( MS62 . MDGCM AS INTEGER ) AS GENMBRID ,
'*OMN' AS SUBACCT ,
MBR01 . MFMNAM AS MBRNAME ,
MBR01B . MFMNAM AS GENMBRNAME ,
MS62 . MDACCT AS ACCTYPE ,
( SUM ( MS62 . MMGNMM ) * ( - 1 ) ) AS MTM ,
0 AS VAR_MAR ,
NOW ( )
FROM I400DTAST . MTSMGNF20F MS62
INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01 ON MS62 . MCDMBR = MBR01 . MEXMEM
INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01B ON MS62 . MDGCM = MBR01B . MEXMEM
GROUP BY MS62 . MCDMBR , MS62 . MDGCM , MS62 . MDACCT , MBR01 . MFMNAM , MBR01B . MFMNAM , MS62 . MDSUB
ORDER BY MS62 . MCDMBR , MS62 . MDACCT ; END 
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSESMAI" (IN IN_STID INTEGER, IN IN_SCENARIO CHARACTER(1))
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC
		DELETE FROM PAMPITE . ESMARPTS WHERE STID = IN_STID AND SCENARIO = IN_SCENARIO ;
	INSERT INTO PAMPITE . ESMARPTS ( STID , SCENARIO , MBRID , GENMBRID , SUBACCT , MBRNAME , GENMBRNAME , ACCTYPE , MTM , VAR_MAR , UPDDATE )
	SELECT IN_STID , IN_SCENARIO , MTM . * , 0 , NOW ( ) FROM ( SELECT BK . MGMBRID AS MBRID , BK . MGGCMID AS GENMBRID , BK . MGSUBACT AS SUBACCOUNT , MBR01 . MFMNAM AS MBRNAME , MBR01B . MFMNAM AS GENMBRNAME , BK . MGACCT AS ACCTYPE , SUM ( BK . MGPRMTM ) AS MTM
	FROM I400DTAST . BKMS2200F BK
	INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01 ON BK . MGMBRID = MBR01 . MEXMEM
	INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01B ON BK . MGGCMID = MBR01B . MEXMEM
	WHERE MGSTLG = 'IDEX' AND MGMGNID = 'O'
	GROUP BY BK . MGMBRID , BK . MGGCMID , MBR01 . MFMNAM , MBR01B . MFMNAM , BK . MGACCT , BK . MGSUBACT
	ORDER BY BK . MGMBRID , BK . MGACCT ) AS MTM ;
	MERGE INTO ESMARPTS A USING ( SELECT IN_STID AS STID , IN_SCENARIO AS SCENARIO , C . MBRID , C . GMBRID , C . MBRNAME , C . GENMBRNAME , C . ACCTYPE , C . SUBACCT , SUM ( C . MTM ) AS VAR_MAR FROM
(
SELECT MTG5 . D14_MBR AS MBRID , MK . MKGCMID AS GMBRID , MBR01 . MFMNAM AS MBRNAME , MBR01B . MFMNAM AS GENMBRNAME , MTG5 . D14_ACCT AS ACCTYPE , TRIM ( MTG5 . D14_SUBAC ) AS SUBACCT ,
CASE WHEN MTG5 . D14_DBTCRD = 'C' THEN - ( MTG5 . D14_MARGIN ) ELSE ( MTG5 . D14_MARGIN ) END AS MTM
FROM I400DTAST . BKMT5500F MTG5
INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01 ON MTG5 . D14_MBR = MBR01 . MEXMEM
INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMMKT00F MK ON MTG5 . D14_MBR = MK . MKMBRID AND MK . MKMKTID = 5
INNER JOIN I400DTAST . CGMBR01L MBR01B ON MK . MKGCMID = MBR01B . MEXMEM ) AS C
GROUP BY C . MBRID , C . GMBRID , C . MBRNAME , C . GENMBRNAME , C . ACCTYPE , C . SUBACCT
ORDER BY C . MBRID , C . GMBRID , C . ACCTYPE , C . SUBACCT ) B ON ( A . STID = B . STID AND A . SCENARIO = B . SCENARIO AND A . MBRID = B . MBRID AND A . GENMBRID = B . GMBRID AND A . SUBACCT = B . SUBACCT AND A . ACCTYPE = B . ACCTYPE )
	WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET A . VAR_MAR = B . VAR_MAR , A . UPDDATE = NOW ( )
	WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN INSERT ( STID , SCENARIO , MBRID , GENMBRID , SUBACCT , MBRNAME , GENMBRNAME , ACCTYPE , MTM , VAR_MAR ) VALUES ( B . STID , B . SCENARIO , B . MBRID , B . GMBRID , B . SUBACCT , B . MBRNAME , B . GENMBRNAME , B . ACCTYPE , 0 , B . VAR_MAR ) ;
END 
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSIRCURV" ()
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC

DECLARE SQLSTATE CHAR ( 5 ) DEFAULT '00000' ;
DECLARE COUNTER INT DEFAULT 0 ;
DECLARE IRNODE INT ;
DECLARE IRNODEDESC VARCHAR ( 255 ) ;
DECLARE LISTNAME VARCHAR ( 255 ) ;
DECLARE INSTRID INT ;
DECLARE INSTRIDCHECK INT DEFAULT 0 ;
DECLARE PRICEDATE TIMESTAMP ;
DECLARE CLOSEPR DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE STATUS CHAR ( 1 ) ;
DECLARE AVE20COEFF DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0.1 ;
DECLARE AVE250COEFF DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0.01 ;
DECLARE AVE20 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE AVE250 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE LASTAVE20 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE LASTAVE250 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE STD20 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE STD250 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE LASTSTD20 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE LASTSTD250 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;

DECLARE INSTRCUR CURSOR FOR
SELECT I . IRNODE , I . IRNODEDESC , I . LISTNAME , P . INSTRID , P . PRICEDATE , P . CLOSEPR , P . STATUS
FROM PAMPITE . PMPTINSTR I
INNER JOIN PAMPITE . PMPTHISPR P ON P . INSTRID = I . INSTRID AND P . PRICEDATE > TIMESTAMP ( CONCAT ( ( YEAR ( NOW ( ) ) - 3 ) , '-01-01 00:00:00.000000' ) )
WHERE I . DIVISCODE = 'B' AND I . INTERP != 'T'
ORDER BY I . INSTRID , P . PRICEDATE ;

DELETE FROM PAMPITE . PMPTIRCURV ;

OPEN INSTRCUR ;

FETCH INSTRCUR INTO IRNODE , IRNODEDESC , LISTNAME , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , CLOSEPR , STATUS ;

WHILE ( SQLSTATE = '00000' ) DO
IF INSTRIDCHECK != INSTRID THEN
SET AVE20 = CLOSEPR ;
SET AVE250 = CLOSEPR ;
SET STD20 = CLOSEPR - AVE20 ;
SET STD250 = CLOSEPR - AVE250 ;	
SET INSTRIDCHECK = INSTRID ;
SET COUNTER = 1 ;
	
ELSE
SET AVE20 = AVE20COEFF * CLOSEPR + ( 1 - AVE20COEFF ) * LASTAVE20 ;
SET AVE250 = AVE250COEFF * CLOSEPR + ( 1 - AVE250COEFF ) * LASTAVE250 ;
SET STD20 = AVE20COEFF * ( CLOSEPR - AVE20 ) + ( 1 - AVE20COEFF ) * LASTSTD20 ;
SET STD250 = AVE250COEFF * ( CLOSEPR - AVE250 ) + ( 1 - AVE250COEFF ) * LASTSTD250 ;
SET COUNTER = COUNTER + 1 ;
END IF ;

SET LASTAVE20 = AVE20 ;
SET LASTAVE250 = AVE250 ;

SET LASTSTD20 = STD20 ;
SET LASTSTD250 = STD250 ;
			

INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTIRCURV ( IRNODE , IRNODEDESC , LISTNAME , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , CLOSEPR , STATUS , NUMBER , AVE20 , AVE250 , STD20 , STD250 )
VALUES ( IRNODE , IRNODEDESC , LISTNAME , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , CLOSEPR , STATUS , COUNTER , AVE20 , AVE250 , STD20 , STD250 ) ;

FETCH INSTRCUR INTO IRNODE , IRNODEDESC , LISTNAME , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , CLOSEPR , STATUS ;
END WHILE ;

CLOSE INSTRCUR ;
END 
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSIRCURV2" ()
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC

DECLARE SQLSTATE CHAR ( 5 ) DEFAULT '00000' ;

DECLARE COUNTER INT DEFAULT 0 ;
DECLARE IRNODE INT ;
DECLARE IRNODEDESC VARCHAR ( 255 ) ;
DECLARE LISTNAME VARCHAR ( 255 ) ;
DECLARE INSTRID INT ;
DECLARE INSTRIDCHECK INT DEFAULT 0 ;
DECLARE PRICEDATE TIMESTAMP ;
DECLARE CLOSEPR DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE STATUS CHAR ( 1 ) ;
DECLARE AVE20COEFF DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0.1 ;
DECLARE AVE250COEFF DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0.01 ;
DECLARE AVE20 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE AVE250 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE LASTAVE20 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE LASTAVE250 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE STD20 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE STD250 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE LASTSTD20 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;
DECLARE LASTSTD250 DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) ;

DECLARE INSTRCUR CURSOR FOR
SELECT I . IRNODE , I . IRNODEDESC , I . LISTNAME , P . INSTRID , P . PRICEDATE , P . CLOSEPR , P . STATUS
FROM PAMPUSE . PMPTINSTR I
INNER JOIN PAMPUSE . PMPTHISPR P ON P . INSTRID = I . INSTRID AND P . PRICEDATE > TIMESTAMP ( CONCAT ( ( YEAR ( NOW ( ) ) - 3 ) , '-01-01 00:00:00.000000' ) )
WHERE I . DIVISCODE = 'B' AND I . INTERP != 'T'
ORDER BY I . INSTRID , P . PRICEDATE ;

DELETE FROM PAMPUSE . PMPTIRCURV ;

OPEN INSTRCUR ;

FETCH INSTRCUR INTO IRNODE , IRNODEDESC , LISTNAME , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , CLOSEPR , STATUS ;

WHILE ( SQLSTATE = '00000' ) DO
IF INSTRIDCHECK != INSTRID THEN
SET AVE20 = CLOSEPR ;
SET AVE250 = CLOSEPR ;
SET STD20 = CLOSEPR - AVE20 ;
SET STD250 = CLOSEPR - AVE250 ;	
SET INSTRIDCHECK = INSTRID ;
SET COUNTER = 1 ;
	
ELSE
SET AVE20 = AVE20COEFF * CLOSEPR + ( 1 - AVE20COEFF ) * LASTAVE20 ;
SET AVE250 = AVE250COEFF * CLOSEPR + ( 1 - AVE250COEFF ) * LASTAVE250 ;
SET STD20 = AVE20COEFF * ( CLOSEPR - AVE20 ) + ( 1 - AVE20COEFF ) * LASTSTD20 ;
SET STD250 = AVE250COEFF * ( CLOSEPR - AVE250 ) + ( 1 - AVE250COEFF ) * LASTSTD250 ;
SET COUNTER = COUNTER + 1 ;
END IF ;

SET LASTAVE20 = AVE20 ;
SET LASTAVE250 = AVE250 ;

SET LASTSTD20 = STD20 ;
SET LASTSTD250 = STD250 ;
			

INSERT INTO PAMPUSE . PMPTIRCURV ( IRNODE , IRNODEDESC , LISTNAME , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , CLOSEPR , STATUS , NUMBER , AVE20 , AVE250 , STD20 , STD250 )
VALUES ( IRNODE , IRNODEDESC , LISTNAME , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , CLOSEPR , STATUS , COUNTER , AVE20 , AVE250 , STD20 , STD250 ) ;

FETCH INSTRCUR INTO IRNODE , IRNODEDESC , LISTNAME , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , CLOSEPR , STATUS ;
END WHILE ;

CLOSE INSTRCUR ;
END 
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSMBTBRC" (IN IN_BTID INTEGER, IN IN_CLASSID INTEGER)
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC

		
		--
		--DECLARE BRC_CNT INT DEFAULT 0;

		/*SQL state = End Of File*/
DECLARE SQLSTATE CHAR ( 5 ) DEFAULT '00000' ;
		
		/*Counters variables*/
		DECLARE WHILE_CNT INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE TOT_BR INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE WRK_BR INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE ADJ_BR INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		
		/*Field variables (previous values)*/
		DECLARE PREV_COUNTER INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PREV_USER_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PREV_ADJST_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PREV_WORK_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PREV_SUP_TH DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PREV_INF_TH DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;
		
		/*Field variables (current values)*/
		DECLARE CURR_COUNTER INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE CURR_BREACH_TYPE CHAR ( 1 ) ;
		DECLARE CURR_SUP_TH DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE CURR_INF_TH DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE CURR_BT_COV DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;	
		DECLARE CURR_USER_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE CURR_ADJST_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE CURR_WORK_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		
		/*Primary key variables*/
		DECLARE NV_VAR INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE INSTR_ID INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PRICE_DATE TIMESTAMP ;
		
		/*Calculated variables*/
		DECLARE USER_DAYS INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
			
		/*Cursor on MIC Breach*/
		DECLARE BTCURSOR CURSOR FOR
			SELECT NV , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , IFNULL ( INFTH , 0 ) , COUNTER , BREACHTY FROM PMPTMSMBRC WHERE BTID = IN_BTID AND CLASSID = IN_CLASSID
			ORDER BY INFTH DESC ;

		/*Set USER_DAYS as Record Count of MIC Breach*/
SELECT COUNT ( BTID ) INTO USER_DAYS FROM PMPTMSMBRC WHERE BTID = IN_BTID AND CLASSID = IN_CLASSID ;
		
		/*Open and fetch the cursor on MIC Breach*/
		OPEN BTCURSOR ;
		FETCH BTCURSOR INTO NV_VAR , INSTR_ID , PRICE_DATE , CURR_INF_TH , CURR_COUNTER , CURR_BREACH_TYPE ;
		
		WHILE ( SQLSTATE = '00000' ) DO

			/*se sto iniziando a contare allora metto tutti i valori a zero e un supth altissimo*/
			IF WHILE_CNT = 0 THEN
				SET CURR_SUP_TH = 1000000.0 ;
				SET CURR_COUNTER = 0 ;
				SET CURR_USER_BRCH = 0 ;
				SET CURR_ADJST_BRCH = 0 ;
				SET CURR_WORK_BRCH = 0 ;
			ELSE
				IF ( PREV_INF_TH = CURR_INF_TH ) THEN
					
					SET CURR_SUP_TH = PREV_SUP_TH ;
					SET CURR_COUNTER = PREV_COUNTER + 1 ;
					SET CURR_USER_BRCH = PREV_USER_BRCH ;
					SET CURR_ADJST_BRCH = PREV_ADJST_BRCH ;
					SET CURR_WORK_BRCH = PREV_WORK_BRCH ;
				
				ELSE
				
					SET CURR_SUP_TH = PREV_INF_TH ;
					SET CURR_COUNTER = 0 ;
					SET CURR_USER_BRCH = TOT_BR ;
					SET CURR_ADJST_BRCH = ADJ_BR ;
					SET CURR_WORK_BRCH = WRK_BR ;
				
				END IF ;
			
			
			END IF ;
			
			--CALCOLO COVERAGE
			SET CURR_BT_COV = 1.0 - ( CURR_USER_BRCH * 1.00 / USER_DAYS ) ;
			
			--UPDATE RIGA
			UPDATE PMPTMSMBRC
				SET USRDAYS = USER_DAYS , USRCOV = CURR_BT_COV , USRBRCH = CURR_USER_BRCH , WRKBRCH = CURR_WORK_BRCH , ADJBRCH = CURR_ADJST_BRCH , SUPTH = CURR_SUP_TH , COUNTER = CURR_COUNTER , UPDDATE = NOW ( )
				WHERE BTID = IN_BTID AND NV = NV_VAR AND CLASSID = IN_CLASSID AND INSTRID = INSTR_ID AND PRICEDATE = PRICE_DATE ;
			
			
			--AGGIORNA CONTATORI TOTBR, WRKBR, ADJBR
			SET TOT_BR = TOT_BR + 1 ;
			SET WHILE_CNT = WHILE_CNT + 1 ;
			IF ( CURR_BREACH_TYPE = 'W' ) THEN
				SET WRK_BR = WRK_BR + 1 ;
			ELSE
				SET ADJ_BR = ADJ_BR + 1 ;
			END IF ;
			
			--AGGIORNA PREVIOUS
			SET PREV_INF_TH = CURR_INF_TH ;
			SET PREV_SUP_TH = CURR_SUP_TH ;
			SET PREV_COUNTER = CURR_COUNTER ;
			SET PREV_USER_BRCH = CURR_USER_BRCH ;
			SET PREV_ADJST_BRCH = CURR_ADJST_BRCH ;
			SET PREV_WORK_BRCH = CURR_WORK_BRCH ;
			
				
			
			FETCH BTCURSOR INTO NV_VAR , INSTR_ID , PRICE_DATE , CURR_INF_TH , CURR_COUNTER , CURR_BREACH_TYPE ;
		END WHILE ;
		
		CLOSE BTCURSOR ;
	END 
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSRESCNT" ()
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC

	DECLARE COUNTER INT DEFAULT 0 ;
	DECLARE SQLSTATE CHAR ( 5 ) DEFAULT '00000' ;
	DECLARE TABLE_NAME VARCHAR ( 255 ) ;
	DECLARE COLUMN_NAME VARCHAR ( 255 ) ;
	DECLARE SQLSTM VARCHAR ( 255 ) ;

	/*Cursor on table count Breach*/
	DECLARE ALTER_CURSOR CURSOR FOR
		SELECT Q . TABLE_NAME , Q . COLUMN_NAME
		FROM QSYS2 . SYSCOLUMNS Q
		WHERE Q . TABLE_SCHEMA = CURRENT SCHEMA
		AND LEFT ( Q . TABLE_NAME , 4 ) IN ( 'PMPT' , 'PMPX' )
		AND Q . IS_IDENTITY = 'YES' ;
		
	/*Open and fetch the cursor on table list*/
	OPEN ALTER_CURSOR ;
	FETCH ALTER_CURSOR INTO TABLE_NAME , COLUMN_NAME ;

	WHILE ( SQLSTATE = '00000' ) DO
		
		SET SQLSTM = 'VALUES (SELECT MAX(' || COLUMN_NAME || ') ' ||
		'FROM ' || TABLE_NAME || ')' || 'INTO ?' ;

		PREPARE S2 FROM SQLSTM ;
		EXECUTE S2 USING COUNTER ;
	
		IF COUNTER IS NULL THEN
			SET COUNTER = 0 ;
		END IF ;
	
		SET COUNTER = COUNTER + 1 ;
			
		SET SQLSTM = 'ALTER TABLE ' || TABLE_NAME || ' ALTER COLUMN ' || COLUMN_NAME || ' RESTART WITH ' || COUNTER ;
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE SQLSTM ;
		
		FETCH ALTER_CURSOR INTO TABLE_NAME , COLUMN_NAME ;

	END WHILE ;

	CLOSE ALTER_CURSOR ;
	
END 
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSSTREP" ()
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC

--IF DIVISCODE = 'E' THEN 
INSERT INTO PMPMSTREP ( INSTRID , CLASSCODE , INSTRNAME , SCENARIO , STID , OLDDATE , LSTHISTDAT , V1 , V2 , SCRES , IMPVOLA , IMPVOLAST )
SELECT I . INSTRID , I . CLASSCODE , I . INSTRNAME , HI . SCENARIO , ST . STID , ST . LSTHISTDAT AS OLDDATE , ST . LSTHISTDAT AS LSTHISTDAT ,
( CASE WHEN HI . CLOSEPR = 0 THEN 0 ELSE - ( HI . CLOSEPR - HI . CLOSEPRST ) / HI . CLOSEPR END ) AS V1 ,
( CASE WHEN HD . CLOSEPR = 0 THEN 0 ELSE - ( HD . CLOSEPR - HD . CLOSEPRST ) / HD . CLOSEPR END ) AS V2 ,
( CASE WHEN HI . CLOSEPR = 0 THEN 0 ELSE - ( HI . CLOSEPR - HI . CLOSEPRST ) / HI . CLOSEPR END ) AS SCRES ,
H . IMPVOLA * 100 AS IMPVOLA , H . IMPVOLAST * 100 AS IMPVOLAST
FROM PMPTINSTR I
INNER JOIN PMPTSTHISP HI ON HI . INSTRID = I . UNDINSTRID
INNER JOIN PMPTSTHISP HD ON HD . INSTRID = I . UNDINSTRID AND HD . STID = HI . STID AND HD . SCENARIO != HI . SCENARIO
INNER JOIN PMPTST ST ON ST . STID = HI . STID AND ST . STID = HD . STID
INNER JOIN PMPTSTHISD H ON H . INSTRID = I . INSTRID AND H . STID = ST . STID AND H . SCENARIO = HI . SCENARIO AND H . ATM = 'T' AND H . PC = 'C'
WHERE (
SELECT COUNT ( * )
FROM PMPTSTHISD H1
WHERE H1 . INSTRID = H . INSTRID AND H1 . EXPIRY < H . EXPIRY AND H1 . STID = H . STID AND H1 . SCENARIO = H . SCENARIO AND H1 . PC = H . PC AND H1 . STRIKE = H . STRIKE
) = 1
AND ST . STID > ( SELECT CASE WHEN MAX ( STID ) IS NOT NULL THEN MAX ( STID ) ELSE 0 END FROM PMPMSTREP WHERE STID IN ( SELECT STID FROM PMPTST WHERE DIVISCODE = 'E' AND STATUS = 'T' ) )
AND ST . STATUS = 'T'
AND I . DIVISCODE = 'D'
ORDER BY ST . LSTHISTDAT ASC ;
--ELSE 
INSERT INTO PMPMSTREP ( INSTRID , CLASSCODE , INSTRNAME , SCENARIO , STID , OLDDATE , LSTHISTDAT , V1 , V2 , SCRES , IMPVOLA , IMPVOLAST )
SELECT I . INSTRID , I . CLASSCODE , I . INSTRNAME , H . SCENARIO , ST . STID , ST . LSTHISTDAT AS OLDDATE , ST . LSTHISTDAT AS LSTHISTDAT , 0 , 0 ,
( CASE WHEN H . CLOSEPR = 0 THEN 0 ELSE - ( H . CLOSEPR - H . CLOSEPRST ) / H . CLOSEPR END ) AS SCRES , 0 , 0
FROM PMPTINSTR I
INNER JOIN PMPTSTHISD H ON I . INSTRID = H . INSTRID
INNER JOIN PMPTST ST ON ST . STID = H . STID
WHERE ST . STID > ( SELECT CASE WHEN MAX ( STID ) IS NOT NULL THEN MAX ( STID ) ELSE 0 END FROM PMPMSTREP WHERE STID IN ( SELECT STID FROM PMPTST WHERE DIVISCODE = 'L' AND STATUS = 'T' ) )
AND ST . STATUS = 'T'
AND I . DIVISCODE = 'L'
ORDER BY ST . LSTHISTDAT ASC ;
--END IF ; 
END 
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE "PAMPITE"."PMPSXBTBRC" (IN IN_BTID INTEGER, IN IN_CLASSID INTEGER)
	LANGUAGE SQL
	DYNAMIC RESULT SETS 0
	NOT DETERMINISTIC
	MODIFIES SQL DATA
	DISALLOW DEBUG MODE
	OLD SAVEPOINT LEVEL
	COMMIT ON RETURN NO
BEGIN ATOMIC

		
		--
		--DECLARE BRC_CNT INT DEFAULT 0;

		/*SQL state = End Of File*/
DECLARE SQLSTATE CHAR ( 5 ) DEFAULT '00000' ;
		
		/*Counters variables*/
		DECLARE WHILE_CNT INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE TOT_BR INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE WRK_BR INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE ADJ_BR INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		
		/*Field variables (previous values)*/
		DECLARE PREV_COUNTER INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PREV_USER_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PREV_ADJST_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PREV_WORK_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PREV_SUP_TH DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PREV_INF_TH DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;
		
		/*Field variables (current values)*/
		DECLARE CURR_COUNTER INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE CURR_BREACH_TYPE CHAR ( 1 ) ;
		DECLARE CURR_SUP_TH DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE CURR_INF_TH DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE CURR_BT_COV DECIMAL ( 15 , 8 ) DEFAULT 0 ;	
		DECLARE CURR_USER_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE CURR_ADJST_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE CURR_WORK_BRCH INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
		
		/*Primary key variables*/
		DECLARE NV_VAR INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE INSTR_ID INT DEFAULT 0 ;
		DECLARE PRICE_DATE TIMESTAMP ;
		
		/*Calculated variables*/
		DECLARE USER_DAYS INTEGER DEFAULT 0 ;
			
		/*Cursor on MIC Breach*/
		DECLARE BTCURSOR CURSOR FOR
			SELECT NV , INSTRID , PRICEDATE , IFNULL ( INFTH , 0 ) , COUNTER , BREACHTY FROM PMPTXSMBRC WHERE BTID = IN_BTID AND CLASSID = IN_CLASSID
			ORDER BY INFTH DESC ;

		/*Set USER_DAYS as Record Count of MIC Breach*/
SELECT COUNT ( BTID ) INTO USER_DAYS FROM PMPTXSMBRC WHERE BTID = IN_BTID AND CLASSID = IN_CLASSID ;
		
		/*Open and fetch the cursor on MIC Breach*/
		OPEN BTCURSOR ;
		FETCH BTCURSOR INTO NV_VAR , INSTR_ID , PRICE_DATE , CURR_INF_TH , CURR_COUNTER , CURR_BREACH_TYPE ;
		
		WHILE ( SQLSTATE = '00000' ) DO

			/*se sto iniziando a contare allora metto tutti i valori a zero e un supth altissimo*/
			IF WHILE_CNT = 0 THEN
				SET CURR_SUP_TH = 1000000.0 ;
				SET CURR_COUNTER = 0 ;
				SET CURR_USER_BRCH = 0 ;
				SET CURR_ADJST_BRCH = 0 ;
				SET CURR_WORK_BRCH = 0 ;
			ELSE
				IF ( PREV_INF_TH = CURR_INF_TH ) THEN
					
					SET CURR_SUP_TH = PREV_SUP_TH ;
					SET CURR_COUNTER = PREV_COUNTER + 1 ;
					SET CURR_USER_BRCH = PREV_USER_BRCH ;
					SET CURR_ADJST_BRCH = PREV_ADJST_BRCH ;
					SET CURR_WORK_BRCH = PREV_WORK_BRCH ;
				
				ELSE
				
					SET CURR_SUP_TH = PREV_INF_TH ;
					SET CURR_COUNTER = 0 ;
					SET CURR_USER_BRCH = TOT_BR ;
					SET CURR_ADJST_BRCH = ADJ_BR ;
					SET CURR_WORK_BRCH = WRK_BR ;
				
				END IF ;
			
			
			END IF ;
			
			--CALCOLO COVERAGE
			SET CURR_BT_COV = 1.0 - ( CURR_USER_BRCH * 1.00 / USER_DAYS ) ;
			
			--UPDATE RIGA
			UPDATE PMPTXSMBRC
				SET USRDAYS = USER_DAYS , USRCOV = CURR_BT_COV , USRBRCH = CURR_USER_BRCH , WRKBRCH = CURR_WORK_BRCH , ADJBRCH = CURR_ADJST_BRCH , SUPTH = CURR_SUP_TH , COUNTER = CURR_COUNTER , UPDDATE = NOW ( )
				WHERE BTID = IN_BTID AND NV = NV_VAR AND CLASSID = IN_CLASSID AND INSTRID = INSTR_ID AND PRICEDATE = PRICE_DATE ;
			
			
			--AGGIORNA CONTATORI TOTBR, WRKBR, ADJBR
			SET TOT_BR = TOT_BR + 1 ;
			SET WHILE_CNT = WHILE_CNT + 1 ;
			IF ( CURR_BREACH_TYPE = 'W' ) THEN
				SET WRK_BR = WRK_BR + 1 ;
			ELSE
				SET ADJ_BR = ADJ_BR + 1 ;
			END IF ;
			
			--AGGIORNA PREVIOUS
			SET PREV_INF_TH = CURR_INF_TH ;
			SET PREV_SUP_TH = CURR_SUP_TH ;
			SET PREV_COUNTER = CURR_COUNTER ;
			SET PREV_USER_BRCH = CURR_USER_BRCH ;
			SET PREV_ADJST_BRCH = CURR_ADJST_BRCH ;
			SET PREV_WORK_BRCH = CURR_WORK_BRCH ;
			
				
			
			FETCH BTCURSOR INTO NV_VAR , INSTR_ID , PRICE_DATE , CURR_INF_TH , CURR_COUNTER , CURR_BREACH_TYPE ;
		END WHILE ;
		
		CLOSE BTCURSOR ;
	END 
GO

CREATE TRIGGER "PAMPITE"."PMPZCONFDF_ARCHIVE_C"
	AFTER INSERT ON "PAMPITE"."PMPTCONFDF"
	REFERENCING NEW AS NROW 
	FOR EACH ROW MODE DB2ROW
	INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPXCONFDF ( INSTRTYPE , NDAYSPER , NV , UPDTYPE , UPDUSR , UPDDATE , CONFIDDF ) VALUES ( NROW . INSTRTYPE , NROW . NDAYSPER , NROW . NV , NROW . UPDTYPE , NROW . UPDUSR , NROW . UPDDATE , NROW . CONFIDDF ) 
GO
CREATE TRIGGER "PAMPITE"."PMPZTYP_DEFAULT_C"
	AFTER INSERT ON "PAMPITE"."PMPTTYP"
	REFERENCING NEW AS NROW 
	FOR EACH ROW MODE DB2ROW
	BEGIN ATOMIC -- INSERIMENTO STATI DELTA DI DEFAULT 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTDELTDF ( INSTRTYPE , NV , DSTATUS ) SELECT NROW . INSTRTYPE , T . NV , 'E' AS DSTATUS FROM PAMPITE . PMPTDELTA T ; -- INSERIMENTO STATI PERIOD DI DEFAULT 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTPERDF ( INSTRTYPE , NDAYSPER , PSTATUS ) SELECT NROW . INSTRTYPE , T . NDAYSPER , 'E' ASPSTATUS FROM PAMPITE . PMPTPER T ; -- INSERIMENTO DEFAULT CONFIDENCE 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTCONFDF ( INSTRTYPE , NDAYSPER , NV , CONFIDDF ) SELECT NROW . INSTRTYPE , P . NDAYSPER , D . NV , 0.99 FROM PAMPITE . PMPTDELTA D , PAMPITE . PMPTPER P ; END 
GO
CREATE TRIGGER "PAMPITE"."PMPZDELTDF_ARCHIVE_C"
	AFTER INSERT ON "PAMPITE"."PMPTDELTDF"
	REFERENCING NEW AS NROW 
	FOR EACH ROW MODE DB2ROW
	INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPXDELTDF ( INSTRTYPE , NV , DSTATUS , UPDTYPE , UPDUSR , UPDDATE ) VALUES ( NROW . INSTRTYPE , NROW . NV , NROW . DSTATUS , NROW . UPDTYPE , NROW . UPDUSR , NROW . UPDDATE ) 
GO
CREATE TRIGGER "PAMPITE"."PMPZGROUP_ARCHIVE_U"
	AFTER UPDATE ON "PAMPITE"."PMPTGROUP"
	REFERENCING OLD AS OROW NEW AS NROW 
	FOR EACH ROW MODE DB2ROW
	BEGIN ATOMIC INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPXGROUP ( GRNAME , INIVDATE , ENDVDATE , SENDDATE , RCCODE , COMMENT , STATUS , USERCOEFF , ANDATE , ANCOEFF , ANNDAYSPER , ANNV , ANVARTYPE , PROPOSE , PROPCOEFF , APPROVAL , UPDTYPE , UPDDATE , UPDUSR , GRID , CRNDAYSPER , CRCOEFF , CRNV , CRVARTYPE , CRLOG , ANLOG , PROPLOG , DIVISCODE ) VALUES ( NROW . GRNAME , NROW . INIVDATE , NROW . ENDVDATE , NROW . SENDDATE , NROW . RCCODE , NROW . COMMENT , NROW . STATUS , NROW . USERCOEFF , NROW . ANDATE , NROW . ANCOEFF , NROW . ANNDAYSPER , NROW . ANNV , NROW . ANVARTYPE , NROW . PROPOSE , NROW . PROPCOEFF , NROW . APPROVAL , NROW . UPDTYPE , NROW . UPDDATE , NROW . UPDUSR , NROW . GRID , NROW . CRNDAYSPER , NROW . CRCOEFF , NROW . CRNV , NROW . CRVARTYPE , NROW . CRLOG , NROW . ANLOG , NROW . PROPLOG , NROW . DIVISCODE ) ; END 
GO
CREATE TRIGGER "PAMPITE"."PMPZSTHISD2_ARCHIVE_C"
	AFTER INSERT ON "PAMPITE"."PMPTSTHISD"
	REFERENCING NEW AS NROW 
	FOR EACH ROW MODE DB2ROW
	IF NROW . CODE = '' THEN
	UPDATE PAMPITE . PMPTSTHISD SET SENT = 'T' WHERE PAMPITE . PMPTSTHISD . INSTRID = NROW . INSTRID AND PAMPITE . PMPTSTHISD . STID = NROW . STID AND PAMPITE . PMPTSTHISD . SCENARIO = NROW . SCENARIO AND PAMPITE . PMPTSTHISD . EXPIRY = NROW . EXPIRY ;
	END IF 
GO

CREATE TRIGGER "PAMPITE"."PMPZSMCONF_UPDATE"
	INSTEAD OF UPDATE ON "PAMPITE"."PMPVSMCONF"
	REFERENCING OLD AS O NEW AS N 
	FOR EACH ROW MODE DB2SQL
	BEGIN ATOMIC IF N . CONFIDENCE = O . CONFIDENCE THEN UPDATE PAMPITE . PMPTSMCONF T SET UNCEVSEL = N . UNCEV , STATUS = N . STATUS WHERE T . INSTRID = N . INSTRID AND T . NV = N . NV AND T . NDAYSPER = N . NDAYSPER ; ELSE UPDATE PAMPITE . PMPTSMCONF T SET CONFIDENCE = N . CONFIDENCE WHERE T . INSTRID = N . INSTRID AND T . NV = N . NV AND T . NDAYSPER = N . NDAYSPER AND T . UNCEV = N . UNCEV ; END IF ; END 
GO

CREATE TRIGGER "PAMPITE"."PMPZDELTA_DEFAULT_C"
	AFTER INSERT ON "PAMPITE"."PMPTDELTA"
	REFERENCING NEW AS NROW 
	FOR EACH ROW MODE DB2ROW
	BEGIN ATOMIC -- INSERIMENTO STATI DELTA DI DEFAULT 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTDELTDF ( INSTRTYPE , NV , DSTATUS ) SELECT T . INSTRTYPE , NROW . NV , 'E' AS DSTATUS FROM PAMPITE . PMPTTYP T ; -- INSERIMENTO DEFAULT CONFIDENCE 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTCONFDF ( INSTRTYPE , NDAYSPER , NV , CONFIDDF ) SELECT T . INSTRTYPE , P . NDAYSPER , NROW . NV , 0.99 FROM PAMPITE . PMPTTYP T , PAMPITE . PMPTPER P ; -- INSERIMENTO CONFIDENCE 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTCONF ( INSTRID , NDAYSPER , NV , STATUS , CONFIDENCE , DEFCONF ) SELECT T . INSTRID , P . NDAYSPER , NROW . NV , 'E' AS STATUS , 0.99 AS CONFIDENCE , 'T' ASDEFCONF FROM PAMPITE . PMPTINSTR T , PAMPITE . PMPTPER P ; -- INSERIMENTO SET PARAMETERS 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTSETPAR ( NDAYSPER , NV , SETID , PSTATUS ) SELECT P . NDAYSPER , NROW . NV , S . SETID , 'E' FROM PAMPITE . PMPTPER P , PAMPITE . PMPTSETS S ; -- INSERIMENTO STRADDLE CORR DEFAULT 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTSTRCDF ( NDAYSPER , NV , STATUS ) SELECT P . NDAYSPER , NROW . NV , 'E' FROM PAMPITE . PMPTPER P ; --INSERIMENTO OFFSETPAR DI DEFAULT 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTOFFPAR ( NDAYSPER , NV , PSTATUS ) SELECT P . NDAYSPER , NROW . NV , 'E' FROM PAMPITE . PMPTPER P ; END 
GO

	END IF

CREATE TRIGGER "PAMPITE"."PMPZINSTR_UPD_FE"
	AFTER UPDATE ON "PAMPITE"."PMPTINSTR"
	REFERENCING OLD AS OROW NEW AS NROW 
	FOR EACH ROW MODE DB2ROW
	BEGIN ATOMIC

IF (
( OROW . INSTRTYPE = 'FE' ) AND (
( OROW . CLASSCODE != NROW . CLASSCODE ) OR
( OROW . UNDINSTRID != NROW . UNDINSTRID ) OR
( OROW . STATUS != NROW . STATUS )
)
) THEN
UPDATE PAMPITE . PMPTINSTR
SET CLASSCODE = NROW . CLASSCODE , STATUS = NROW . STATUS , UNDINSTRID = NROW . UNDINSTRID
WHERE PAMPITE . PMPTINSTR . CLASSCODE = OROW . CLASSCODE AND PAMPITE . PMPTINSTR . INSTRID != OROW . INSTRID AND PAMPITE . PMPTINSTR . INSTRTYPE = 'FE' ;
END IF ;
END 
GO
CREATE TRIGGER "PAMPITE"."PMPZPER_DEFAULT_C"
	AFTER INSERT ON "PAMPITE"."PMPTPER"
	REFERENCING NEW AS NROW 
	FOR EACH ROW MODE DB2ROW
	BEGIN ATOMIC -- INSERIMENTO STATI PERIODO DI DEFAULT 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTPERDF ( INSTRTYPE , NDAYSPER , PSTATUS ) SELECT T . INSTRTYPE , NROW . NDAYSPER , 'E' ASPSTATUS FROM PAMPITE . PMPTTYP T ; -- INSERIMENTO DEFAULT CONFIDENCE 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTCONFDF ( INSTRTYPE , NDAYSPER , NV , CONFIDDF ) SELECT T . INSTRTYPE , NROW . NDAYSPER , D . NV , 0.99 FROM PAMPITE . PMPTTYP T , PAMPITE . PMPTDELTA D ; -- INSERIMENTO CONFIDENCE 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTCONF ( INSTRID , NDAYSPER , NV , STATUS , CONFIDENCE , DEFCONF ) SELECT T . INSTRID , NROW . NDAYSPER , D . NV , 'E' AS STATUS , 0.99 AS CONFIDENCE , 'T' ASDEFCONF FROM PAMPITE . PMPTINSTR T , PAMPITE . PMPTDELTA D ; -- INSERIMENTO SET PARAMETERS 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTSETPAR ( NDAYSPER , NV , SETID , PSTATUS ) SELECT NROW . NDAYSPER , D . NV , S . SETID , 'E' FROM PAMPITE . PMPTDELTA D , PAMPITE . PMPTSETS S ; -- INSERIMENTO STRADDLE CORRELATION DEFAULT 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTSTRCDF ( NDAYSPER , NV , STATUS ) SELECT NROW . NDAYSPER , D . NV , 'E' FROM PAMPITE . PMPTDELTA D ; --INSERIMENTO OFFSET PAR DEFAULT 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTOFFPAR ( NDAYSPER , NV , PSTATUS ) SELECT NROW . NDAYSPER , D . NV , 'E' AS PSTATUS FROM PAMPITE . PMPTDELTA D ; END 
GO
CREATE TRIGGER "PAMPITE"."PMPZINSTR_DEFAULT_C"
	AFTER INSERT ON "PAMPITE"."PMPTINSTR"
	REFERENCING NEW AS NROW 
	FOR EACH ROW MODE DB2ROW
	BEGIN ATOMIC -- INSERIMENTO CONFIDENCE 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTCONF ( INSTRID , NDAYSPER , NV , STATUS , CONFIDENCE , DEFCONF ) SELECT NROW . INSTRID , T . NDAYSPER , T . NV , 'E' AS STATUS , T . CONFIDDF AS CONFIDENCE , 'T' AS DEFCONF FROM PAMPITE . PMPTCONFDF T WHERE T . INSTRTYPE = NROW . INSTRTYPE ; -- INSERIMENTO VALORI NELLA TABELLA DITRASCODIFICA 
INSERT INTO PAMPITE . PMPTTRSINS ( INSTRID , SICINSTR , SICINSTRTY ) SELECT I . INSTRID , I . CLASSCODE , T . SICINSTRTY FROM PAMPITE . PMPTINSTR I INNER JOIN PAMPITE . PMPTTRSCOD T ON I . INSTRTYPE = T . INSTRTYPE WHERE NROW . INSTRID = I . INSTRID AND I . CLASSCODE IS NOT NULL AND T . SICINSTRTY IS NOT NULL ; END 
GO
